Jeremia 1:1 Man lok pa Jeremia wod pa Ilkia, ma en ŋat acel i kin ajwagi ma yam onoŋo gibedo i Anatot i lobo pa Benjamin.
Jeremia 1:2 Lok pa Rwot obino bote i mwaka me apar wiye adek me loc pa Yocia wod pa Amon, kabaka me Juda.
Jeremia 1:3 Lokke obino bene bote i kare me loc pa Yekoyakim wod pa Yocia kabaka me Juda, o kwede wa i agikki mwaka me apar wiye acel me loc pa Jedekia, wod pa Yocia, kabaka me Juda, o wa i kare ma doŋ gitero kwede jo Jerucalem woko i opii i dwe me abic.
Jeremia 1:4 I kare meno lok pa Rwot obino bota ma wacci,
Jeremia 1:5 “I kare ma onoŋo peya acweyi i i meni onoŋo doŋ aŋeyi, dok i kare ma peya ginywali onoŋo doŋ atyeko kweri woko ibed leŋ pi ticca, ayeri me bedo lanebi bot rok ducu,”
Jeremia 1:6 Ka doŋ agamo lokke kun awaco ni, “Aya, Rwot Lubaŋa! Nen, an pe aŋeyo lok, pien an pud latin mamwa.”
Jeremia 1:7 Ento Rwot odok iye owacca ni, “Pe iwacci, ‘An latin mamwa’; pien ibicito bot jo ducu ma abicwali ni icit botgi, dok bene gin ma an abiciki kwede en aye in ibiloko.
Jeremia 1:8 Pe ibed ki lworo mo i komgi, pien atye kwedi, abilari, man Rwot ma owaco.”
Jeremia 1:9 Cutcut Rwot ocwalo ciŋe ogudo doga; ka en Rwot owacca ni, “Nen, doŋ atyeko keto lokka i dogi.
Jeremia 1:10 Nen, doŋ atyeko keti i nino man me loyo rok mapol ki ker mapol, pi putogi ki mukogi wo ko bene, pi balogi ki turogi woko bene, ka gerogi odoco ki ka pitogi bene,”
Jeremia 1:11 Lok pa Rwot dok obino bota ma penya ni, “Jeremia, it ye ka neno aŋo?” Ci agamo ni, “Atye ka neno yat otit.”
Jeremia 1:12 Lacen Rwot owacca ni, “Ineno kara maber, pien atitti ni atye ka neno lokka, amito ni oti ticce ocob kakare.”
Jeremia 1:13 Lok pa Rwot dok obino bota pi tyen me aryone, ma wacci, “It ye ka neno gin aŋo?” An adok iye awacci, “Anene agulu ma pii tye ka walo ki iye, ma doge olokke okemo yo tuŋ acam.”
Jeremia 1:14 Ci Rwot owaco bata ni, “Gin marac bia ki yo tuŋ acam bino poto i kom jo ducu ma gibedo i lobo man.
Jeremia 1:15 Pien nen, atye ka lwoŋo rok ducu ma gitye i te ker ducu ma yo tuŋ acam, gibibino ci ŋat acel acel bicibo komkerre i dog gaŋ me Jerucalem, ma girumo celle woko litit pi lweny i kome, ki pi lweny i kom gaŋi ducu me Juda, Man Rwot ma owaco.
Jeremia 1:16 Dok abiŋolo koppa i kom jo Juda pi timgi maraco ducu ki pi bwota woko; gubedo ka waŋo odok eceta bot lubaŋa mogo mukene, kun gibedo bene ka woro gin ma gutiyo atiya ki ciŋgi.
Jeremia 1:17 Ento in, di cwinyi matek; a malo, ci itit botgi kit gin ducu ma aciki kwede. Cwinyi pe myero oballe i komgi, wek an bene pe abal cwinyi i nyimgi.
Jeremia 1:18 Doŋ inen, atye ka miyo ibedo macalo gaŋ me cel go go matek, macalo wir nyonyo, ki cel mola, pi gwoki i kom jo me lobo man ducu, pi gwoki ki i kom luker me Juda, rwodine, ajwagine, ki i kom lwak ducu me lobo man.
Jeremia 1:19 Gibilweny i komi, ento pe gibitwero loyi, pien an atye kwedi pi lari.” Man lok pa Rwot kikome.
Jeremia 2:1 Lok pa Rwot obino bota ma wacci,
Jeremia 2:2 “Cit ituc lok man bot jo Jerucalem, wek guwiny. Rwot owaco kuman ni, Pud apo pi gen ma ibedo kwede i koma nia ka tinoni, mar ma ibedo kwede macalo nyako ger, kit ma ibedo ka luba kwede wa i dye tim, i lobo ma yam pe gicoyo iye kodi mo.
Jeremia 2:3 Icrael onoŋo yam obedo rok ma gikwero obed maleŋ pi Rwot, macalo cam ma okwoŋo cek ma en okayo. Jo ducu ma gucamo cam meno gulokke gudoko lubal; gin maraco obino opoto i komgi, man Rwot ma owaco.”
Jeremia 2:4 Wuwiny lok pa Rwot, wun jo me ot pa Yakobo, ki wun jo me doggola ducu me ot pa Icrael.
Jeremia 2:5 Rwot dok owaco kuman ni, “Kit gin aŋo marac ma kwarowu gunoŋo ni atimo ma omiyo gua woko ki bota gucito woko ka mabor kweda-ni, gubedo ka lubo gin ma konnye pe, omiyo gin bene gudoko jo ma konygi pe-ni?
Jeremia 2:6 Gin pe gupenyo ni, ‘Rwot ma okwanyowa woko ki i lobo Ejipt-ni mono tye kwene, ma otelo wiwa i dye tim, i lobo tim aroo ma tye iye lwak bur mapol, i lobo mutwo ki mutu me colpiny ma ocido licuc, ki lobo ma yam dano mo pe kato ki iye, ka ma dano mo bene pe bedo iye?’
Jeremia 2:7 Ci akelowu i lobo ma ceko cam mabup adada wek wuyom cwinywu kun wucamo cam ma ocek iye ki gin mabeco ducu ma tye iye. Ento i kare ma wubino-ni wubalo lobona woko, wuloko gipinnya odoko gin me kwer.
Jeremia 2:8 Ajwagi bene gupenyo ni, ‘Rwot mono tye kwene?’ Jo ma gin ludiro i cik bene onoŋo pe giŋeya; luloc gutimo roc i koma; lunebi gubedo ka tyeto lok i nyiŋ jok Baal, gubedo ka lubo kor cal jogi ma pe konyo.”
Jeremia 2:9 Rwot owaco ni, “Pud abipenyo dogwu, abipenyo bene wa dog likwayowu.
Jeremia 2:10 Pi meno koŋ iŋol nam ikat loka Caiprac wek inen, nyo koŋ icwal dano ocit i Kedar wek ociŋi maber twatwal; nen ka ce gin ma kit meno yam obedo tye con.
Jeremia 2:11 Tye rok mo ma oloko lubaŋane pi lubaŋa mo mukene, kadi bed onoŋo gin jogi mamwa? Ento jona doŋ guloko Deyogi woko pi gin ma pe konyogi kadi ki acel.
Jeremia 2:12 In polo, bed ki ur pi lok man, bed ma inen, ma lworo obwoyo komi woko adada, man Rwot ma owaco,
Jeremia 2:13 pien jona doŋ gutyeko timo bal aryo maraco; doŋ gubwota woko, kun an aye abedo-wan it me pii me kwo, gin dok gukwinyo taŋi pii megi pigi kengi, taŋi mutur, ma pe twero jolo pii kadi matidi mo.
Jeremia 2:14 “Icrael mono obedo opii? En latic ma ginywalo anywala i paco? En doŋ odoko macalo ginayaka kono niŋniŋ?
Jeremia 2:15 Lwak labwor ducu doŋ gukok woko i kome matek, gubworo kun gikok ki dwangi maloŋo adada. Gubalo lobone woko odoŋ noŋo; gaŋine ducu doŋ gudoko wi obur, laboŋo dano mo ma bedo i igi.
Jeremia 2:16 Medo i kom meno, jo Mempic ki jo Tapanec doŋ guketo ret i wiye woko.
Jeremia 2:17 Pe wun giwu aye ma wukelo can man i komwu kekenwu pi bwoto Rwot Lubaŋawu, i kare ma yam en obedo ka telo yo botwu-ni?
Jeremia 2:18 Doŋ kombeddi ka wucito i Ejipt ci wunoŋo iye kit kony aŋo, kun wucito ka mato pii ma i kulu Nail? Nyo ka wucito i Aciria kono wunoŋo iye kit kony aŋo, kun wucito ka mato pii ma i kulu Euprate?
Jeremia 2:19 Balwu aye bikelo pwod i komwu, ki bwoto Lubaŋa woko aye bikelo can i komwu me jukowu. Wuŋe dok wunen ni man gin marac dok me cwercwiny pi wun me bwoto Rwot Lubaŋawu woko; kit lworo mo ma wulwora kwede pe i iwu wacel, man Rwot Lubaŋa me mony aye ma owaco.
Jeremia 2:20 “Yam con wuturo okolwu woko dok bene wucodo ogwil ma gitwe-yowu kwede woko; ci wuwacci, ‘Pe abibedo laticci.’ Iyo, i wi cere mamalo ducu kadi i te yat ma pote oluk-gu wubedo ka ryebbe piny macalo malaya.
Jeremia 2:21 An yam onoŋo apitowu kun wua ki i kom olok mamit, akwanyowu ki i kom olok ma nyige ducu beco adada. Wun dok wucako lokke niŋniŋ ci wudoko olok me tim-mi?
Jeremia 2:22 Kadi bed wulwok komwu ki cabun magwa kadi bed wulwokke ki cabun ma bwoyone dwoŋ, lwit bal aliiwu noŋo pud odoŋ tye i nyima, man Rwot Lubaŋa ma owaco.
Jeremia 2:23 Wutwero waco niŋniŋ ni, ‘An gira pe anyobbe ki bal, pe bene abedo ka woro jogi Baal’? Koŋ inen ojwe tyeni ma iwoto kwede i luŋ; dok myero iŋe gin ma doŋ itimo. In ibedo calo roya kinaga ma woto lubo yone kene,
Jeremia 2:24 calo kana me tim ma doŋ oŋiyo woko ki bedo i tim, ma ywayo yamo ki ume kun mito twon! Aŋa ma twero juko gin ma cwinye pyette iye? Jo ducu ma giyenye pe myero guol komgi; gibinoŋe i dwene kikome.
Jeremia 2:25 Gwok tyeni pe iwot kwede laboŋo war, ki dwani bene wek pe otwo woko ki orwo pii. Ento in iwaco ni, ‘Pe doŋ konyo, pien doŋ amaro lubaŋa pa lurok, dok bene doŋ abiwoto alubo korgi.’
Jeremia 2:26 “Kit macalo lakwo lewic mako ka ce gimako ka kwalo gin mo, kit meno jo me ot pa Icrael lewic bene bimakogi: gin kikomgi, lukergi, rwodigi, ajwagigi, kadi wa lunebigi,
Jeremia 2:27 ma giwaco ki yat mo-ni ni, ‘In i wora,’ dok giwaco ki got mo-ni ni. ‘In aye ma inywala.’ Pien onoŋo guloko ŋegi woko bota, pe onoŋo ginena ki waŋgi. Ento i kare ma gitye i can giwacci, ‘A malo ilarwa!’
Jeremia 2:28 Ento lwak lubaŋawu-gu, ma wutiyo piwu kenwu gitye kwene? Wek gua malo ka ce gitwero larowu, i kare ma noŋo wutye i can; pien lwak lubaŋawu gipol ma girom aroma ki wel gaŋiwu, Wun jo Juda.”
Jeremia 2:29 Rwot owacci, “Piŋo wuŋur i koma? Wun ducu doŋ onoŋo wujemo woko i koma.
Jeremia 2:30 Yam apwodo litinowu kwe, pe kitgi oyubbe kadi ki acel; pala lucwanwu dano woko.
Jeremia 2:31 Doŋ wun jo me kare man, wuwiny lok pa Rwot. An mono onoŋo abedo macalo tim bot jo Icrael, nyo macalo lobo me mutu? Piŋo kono jona giwacci, ‘Wan wabibedo kit macalo wamito, pe wabibino boti matwal’?
Jeremia 2:32 Wutamo ni nyako mo wiye twero wil i kom ginaruka me deyone, nyo nyako ger wiye twero wil i kom gomcine me nyom? Ento jona wigi owil woko i koma pi lwak nino ma welle pe kwanne.
Jeremia 2:33 “Kit ma dok iŋeyo yo maber me maro kit me tarwaŋ! Kadi wa mon ma kitgi raco in aye ma ipwonyogi ki tim me tarwaŋ.
Jeremia 2:34 Dok bene i kom boŋo ma i pyeri gityeko noŋo iye remo pa lucan ma pe gitye ki bal alii mo; yam bene pe inoŋogi ka turo ot wek gidony iye. Doŋ i kom lok magi
Jeremia 2:35 in iwacci, ‘An ape ki bal mo; adada kinigane doŋ otyeko a woko ki i koma.’ Nen, abiŋolo kop i komi pi waco ni, ‘Pe onoŋo abalo.’
Jeremia 2:36 Piŋo ibedo ka wirre ki wot kun iloko yoni atata! Jo Ejipt gibimiyo lewic maki kit macalo yam jo Aciria guketo lewic i komi-ni.
Jeremia 2:37 Ibia ki kunnu idwogo woko cen ma noŋo idodo ciŋi i wii, pien Rwot doŋ okwero jo ma it ye ka genogi-ni woko, dok gin pe gibikonyi miyo ibedo maber wacel.”
eremia 3:1 Rwot owaco ni, “Ka laco mo oryemo dakone woko, ce dakone oa ki bote ocito woko, ci doŋ odoko dako pa laco mukene, cware mukwoŋo-ni pud dok bidok bot dako-nu? Ci meno pe bimiyo lobo nyobbe woko ki bal twatwal? Ibedoka timotimkwele ki jo mapol; ci dok pud itwero dwogo bota adada?
eremia 3:2 “Tiŋ waŋi malo wek inen cere mutiŋŋe malo mabor-gul Wi cere mene mudoŋ ma pe co obuto kwedi iye? I ŋet yo ducu ibedo ka kuro pacogi ducu ma gimari-ni calo Laarab mo ma bedo i dye tim. Doŋ ibalo lobo woko ki tim kwele kwele me malayani-ni.
eremia 3:3 Mumiyo kadi kot bene doŋ ojukke woko, ki kot me oro ma onoŋo myero ocwer bene doŋ pe; ento tarwaŋ pud omoro waŋi i tim me kwele, ikwero woko ni lewic pe omaki.
eremia 3:4 Pud pe ilwoŋa kombeddi ni, ‘Wora, in ibedo larema nia wa ka tinona’?
eremia 3:5 Kun itamo ni, ‘En pe bibedo ki kiniga i koma nakanaka, pe bibedo ki akeca nio wa i agikki.’ Nen, in doŋ iloko, ento kono doŋ ityeko timo kit bal ducu macalo itwero.”
eremia 3:6 I kare pa kabaka Yocia, Rwot owaco bota ni, “Doŋ ineno gin ma Icrael ma pe genne-ni otiyo, kit macalo obedo ka cito kwede i wi godi maboco ki i te yadi muluk-gu kun timo iye tim kwele kwelene?
eremia 3:7 Abedo ka tamone, ni ‘Ka doŋ en otyeko timo timme ducu ci en bidwogo bota’; ento en pe omed de ki dwogo cen, kadi laminne Juda ma jone lugoba-ni bene oneno.
eremia 3:8 Kadi bed Juda oneno ni laminne Icrael obedo ka timo abor twatwal i nyima, en gin mumiyo yam aryeme woko kun amiyo bote waraga ma nyuto ni doŋ apokke woko kwede, ento Juda lacarcar-ri pe obedo iye ki lworo mo wacel. En bene ocito obedo ka timo tim me kwele kwele.
eremia 3:9 Pien onoŋo tim me kwele obedo gin mayot ki tuŋ bote, omiyo obalo lobo woko ki bedo ka timo abor ki got wa ki yat-gu.
eremia 3:10 Ento pi lok man ducu Juda ma laminne ma lacarcar-ri pe olokke odwogo bota ki cwinye ducu, ento odwogo i nyima ki kome keken, man Rwot ma owaco.”
eremia 3:11 Rwot owacca ni, “Icrael ma pe genne-ni balle nen nok i waŋa kato pa Juda ma jone lugoba-ni.
eremia 3:12 Cit ituc lok magi i but piny yo tuŋ acam, kun iwacci, ‘Dwog cen, in Icrael ma pe genne-ni, man Rwot ma owaco. Pe abineni ki kiniga, pien an lakica mada. Kiniga pe bimaka nakanaka. Man Rwot ma owaco.
eremia 3:13 Ye balli keken, ni ityeko jemo woko i kom Rwot Lubaŋani, ci ikeyo berri woko i kin lubaŋa pa lurok, kun ibedo ka worogi i te yadi ducu muluk-gu, dok bene pe ibedo ka winyo lokka, man Rwot kikome ma owaco.
eremia 3:14 “ ‘Wudwog cen, wun litino ma pe genne, Rwot ma owaco; pien an laditwu; abikwanyowu, kun akwanyo dano acel ki i gaŋ acel acel, ki jo aryo ki i kaka acel acel, ci abikelowu i Cion.
eremia 3:15 “ ‘Abimiyo botwu bene lukwat ma yomo cwinya, wek gukwawu, ma gipitowu kun gitye ki ŋec wa ki niaŋ maber.
eremia 3:16 Ka ce doŋ inen ni wunya i lobo ma welwu omedde i kare meno, man Rwot ma owaco, pe dok gibibedo ka lwoŋo nyiŋ canduk me gicikke pa Rwot. Pe dok wubitamo pire, pe wubipo pire, dok bene pe gibiyubo odoco.
eremia 3:17 I kare meno doŋ gibilwoŋo Jerucalem ni komker pa Rwot, ci rok ducu gibicokke iye i nyim Rwot, kun pe dok gilubo tam maraco i cwinygi matwal, ŋutgi bene pe doŋ bibedo nwaŋ.
eremia 3:18 I kare meno jo me ot pa Juda gibiribbe woko kacel ki jo me ot pa Icrael, ci gibia kacel ki i lobo ma tye yo tuŋ acam gibino i lobo ma yam amiyo bot kwarogi me bedo gipinygi.
eremia 3:19 “ ‘Abedo ka tamo kit macalo abiketowu kwede i kin litinona, kun amiyowu bene lobo ma yomo cwinywu, gipiny maber makato lobo pa rok mukene ducu. Dok abedo ka tamo ni gwok wubilwoŋa ni an a Wonwu, dok ni pe wubilokke wuweko luba.
eremia 3:20 Adada, kit macalo dako ma pe lagen weko kwede cware, wun bene wubedo laboŋo gen i koma kit meno, wun jo me ot pa Icrael, man Rwot ma owaco.’ ”
eremia 3:21 Dwan dano ma kok tye ka winnye ki i wi cere mubedo barbar, kun pido kwede pi litino pa Icrael, pien guŋak woko ki i yogi, wigi doŋ otyeko wil woko i kom Rwot Lubaŋagi.
eremia 3:22 “Wudwog cen bota, wun litino ma wupe ki gen, an aye ma abicaŋo cwinywu ma pe ki gen-ni woko.” “Nen, wabino boti; pien in aye i Rwot Lubaŋawa.
eremia 3:23 Adada kony mo pe ginoŋo ki i wi got ka ma woo pa lwak dano winnye a ki iye- nu. Adada larre pa Icrael tye bot Rwot Lubaŋawa.
eremia 3:24 “Ento cakke wa ka tinowa tim me lewic ocamo gin ducu ma yam kwarowa guyelle pigi, dyegigi ki romigi, dyaŋigi, awobegi ki anyiragi.
eremia 3:25 Weku doŋ wabutu piny ki lewicwa-ni, wek tim maraco me lewic ma watimo aye oum komwa woko; pien doŋ watyeko timo bal i kom Rwot Lubaŋawa, waŋ kacel ki kwarowa, cakke wa ka tinowa o kwede wa onyoo. Dok bene pe wabedo ka lubo lok pa Rwot Lubaŋawa.”
Jeremia 4:1 “Ka ce wudwogo cen bota, wun jo Icrael, man Rwot ma owaco, myero wudwog giwu. Ka ce wukwanyo gin me kwerwu woko ducu ki i nyima, ma pe doŋ wu biŋak woko aye,
Jeremia 4:2 dok bene ka ce wukwoŋo kwoŋ ni, ‘Kit macalo Rwot tye kwe-ni,’ myero wukwoŋ i ada, kun wulubo ŋolo kop atir, dok bene ki leŋcwiny, ci lurok ducu gibilego Rwot wek oony gum mere i komgi, doŋ gibibedo ka miye deyo.”
Jeremia 4:3 Rwot owaco kuman bot jo Juda ki bot jo ma gibedo i Jerucalem ni, “Wucer poto botwu woko maber, pe wuco kit kodi mo i kin okuto.
Jeremia 4:4 Wun doŋ myero wulirre woko pi tiyo tic pa Rwot, wulirre i cwinywu, wun jo Juda kacel ki jo ma wubedo i Jerucalem; wek akemona pe okatti woko ma lyel macalo mac, ma biwaŋo piny woko ma ŋat mo pe romo nekone, pi gin marac ma onoŋo wutimo.”
Jeremia 4:5 Wutit lok man i Juda, kun wutuco pire bene i Jerucalem, ma wuwacci, “Wukut tum wek kokone orom i lobo woko ducu; wudaŋŋe matek kunwuwacci, ‘Wucokke kacel wek wacitu i gaŋi me cel gogo-gu!’
Jeremia 4:6 Wutiŋ benderawu malo wukem Cion, wuriŋ woko wular komwu, pe wubedi, pien amito kelo gin marac ki yo tuŋ acam, ki to-piny madit mada ma neko danotyeko wako.
Jeremia 4:7 Labwor doŋ okatti woko ki i buŋa muculle likuŋ, lanek rok ducu doŋ okatti woko; oa woko ki i kabedone wek ebal lobowu woko odoŋ obur; gaŋiwu ducu doŋ bidoko wi obur laboŋo dano mo ma bedo i igi.
Jeremia 4:8 Pi man wutwe boŋo cola i pyerwu, wukum kun wukok; pien kiniga mager pa Rwot pe olokke oa woko ki i komwa.”
Jeremia 4:9 Rwot owacci, “I nino meno tekcwiny pa luker ki pa rwodi bitum woko; ajwagi bibaŋŋe woko, ki lunebi bene gibiuro matek.”
Jeremia 4:10 Cutcut agamo awacci, “Aya, Rwot Lubaŋa, adada in doŋ ibwolo lwak man ki jo Jerucalem marac mada, kun iwacci, ‘Wubibedo maber ki kuc’; kun doŋ onoŋo imiyo ginekogi woko ki pala lucwan.”
Jeremia 4:11 I kare meno gibiwaco bot lwak man ki bot jo Jerucalem ni, “Yamo malyet oa ki i wi cere ma yadi pe iye ma tye i tim aroo, kun kodo dok kwede yo tuŋ bot lwakka, pe pi pyetogi macalo kal wek gubed maleŋ;
Jeremia 4:12 yamo ma acwalo-ni ger mupoŋ mada, ma pe doŋ romo pyetogi apyeta wek gubed maleŋ, An aye kombeddi ma atye ka lok pi ŋolo kop i komgi.”
Jeremia 4:13 Nen, tye ka bino calo pol, gadigadi lwennye ducu gibedo calo yamo lapiru; aguragurane gidwir giloyo ocur woko. Can i wiwa, pien doŋ wato watum woko matwal!
Jeremia 4:14 Wun jo Jerucalem, myero wulwok cwinywu woko i timo tim maraco, wek wularre. Tamwu maraco-gu bibedo mono i cwinywu pi kare ma rom mene?
Jeremia 4:15 Dwan dano winnye kun a ki i Dan ma tito ki i wi got Epraim pi gin marac ma bitimme.
Jeremia 4:16 Tit lok man bot rok ducu, ni en tye ka bino; tit ki Jerucalem bene ni. “Mony ma rumo gaŋ bino kun gia ki i lobo mabor; gidaŋŋe ki woo mapol i kom gaŋi me Juda.
Jeremia 4:17 Gurumo Juda woko dyere calo lukur poto ma gurumo poto woko litit, pien onoŋo Juda ojemo woko i koma, man Rwot kikome ma owaco.
Jeremia 4:18 Kitwu ki gin ma wutimo ducu aye okelo can man i komwu. Man aye kipwolawu, can makec bene atika; can man oton wa i cwinywu kikome.”
Jeremia 4:19 Arem doŋ omaka woko, omaka woko do! Arem doŋ wano koma adada. Oii, mil wa i pal cwinya kikome! Adunona tye ka gone atata matek lirimrim; pe atwero liŋ wacel; pien abedo ka winyo koko tum ma gikuto, pi oduru me lweny.
Jeremia 4:20 Can madit poto dodde i kom can madit wadi, lobo ducu doŋ gibalo woko, piny odoŋ obur. Gijwero kemana woko oyotoyot mada, gimuko kicikana woko bene pi dakika manok keken.
Jeremia 4:21 Abibedo ka neno bendera pi kare marom mene, kun abedo ka winyo koko tum?
Jeremia 4:22 “Pien jona-gu gin lumiŋ, pe giŋeya; gin litino ma wigi odiŋ, pe gitye ki kit niaŋ mo. Giryek megi i tiyo gin marac keken, ento pe giŋeyo tiyo gin maber.” Can ma bipoto
Jeremia 4:23 Ka aneno lobo, ci aneno oballe woko odoko obur, laboŋo gin mo ma odon iye; ki malo i polo kuca, lakalatwe ki dwe bene pe giryeny.
Jeremia 4:24 Aneno wi godi, ci aneno gitye ka yeŋŋe ayeŋa ni yegeyege, cere-gu noŋo tye ka wirre liwir ma gigwennye agweriya.
Jeremia 4:25 Aneno ci anoao dano mo pe kunnu, winyo me polo ducu gutuk gucito woko.
Jeremia 4:26 Aneno piny, ci anoŋo ni lobo ma yam ceko cam twatwal-li doŋ odoko tim aroo, gaŋi ma i iye ducu doŋ gibalo woko gudoko obur nyim Rwot ma onoŋo kiniga mager omako-ni.
Jeremia 4:27 Pien Rwot onoŋo owaco kuman ni, “Lobo man ducu bidoko obur; ento pe abityekone woko liweŋ.
Jeremia 4:28 Lobo bikumo pi lok man, ki polo bene bicido woko macol licuc. Pien doŋ atyeko tito ka maleŋ gin ma onoŋo ayubbe me timone; kica pe bimaka wacel, dok bene pe abiloko tamma.”
Jeremia 4:29 Jo ma i gaŋ ducu guriŋo woko pi woo pa wegi aguragura ki wegi atero; gudonyo woko i buŋa macol, gucito wa i kin got-gu; gaŋi ducu doŋ gibwoto woko, dano mo pe ma bedo i igi.
Jeremia 4:30 In gaŋ ma doŋ idoko wi obur-ri, piŋo iruko boŋo makwar? Piŋo kono idero komi ki gin me deyo ma obedo jabu jabu, kun iwiro waŋi woko ki raŋi wek onen maber makato? Iyelle noŋo me deyo komi ni onen maber. Pacogi-gu ducu gicayi acaya; giyenyo yo me neki woko.
Jeremia 4:31 Awinyo koko mo ma cal ki koko pa dako ma tye ka rem ki nywal, ma tye ki arem madwoŋ calo dako ma pud nywalo latin kayone anywala, Ci on tye ka koko kun kwitte pi noŋo yweyo, kun ryeyo ciŋe woko ma wacci, “Can i wiya gira! Awille woko i nyim lunek dano.”
Jeremia 5:1 Wurir; kun wugwennye agwenya i dye yo me Jerucalem, wunen ci myero wuniaŋ iye maber! Wuyeny piny i dyekalle ducu wek wunen ka wutwero noŋo dano mo iye ma ŋolo kop kakare, ma yenyo ada bene; ka wek atim kica ki Jerucalem.
Jeremia 5:2 Kadi bed gikwoŋo kwoŋ kun giwacci, “Kit macalo Rwot tye makwo-ni” ento noŋo gikwoŋo kwoŋ me goba goba.
Jeremia 5:3 Ai Rwot, in mono pe iyenyo ni inen ada ki waŋi? Ipwodogi matek, ento pe guwinyo kit arem mo madwoŋ wacel; ityekogi woko bene, ento gin gukwero winyo pwonnyi. Gujiŋo cwinygi odoko matek makato got; gukwero ŋut woko.
Jeremia 5:4 Dok awacci, “Magi lucan keken, pe gitye ki kit ŋec mo; pien pe giŋeyo yo pa Rwot, ma en aye cik pa Lubaŋagi.
Jeremia 5:5 Abicito bot jo madito ma gin wegi twero, ci abiloko kwedgi; pien giŋeyo yo pa Rwot, ma en aye cik pa Lubaŋagi.” Ento gin bene onoŋo guturo okol woko, dok bene onoŋo gucodo ogwil woko.
Jeremia 5:6 Pi meno, labwor mo bia ki i buŋa ci nekogi woko, orudi ma bedo i tim aroo bibino tyekogi woko. Kwac aye ma doŋ tye ka kuro gaŋigi, ŋat mo ki i kingi ka oa
Jeremia 5:7 “Atwero timowu kica niŋniŋ? Litinowu doŋ gubwota woko, kun gubedo ka kwoŋo kwoŋ ki nyiŋ lubaŋa mogo ma pe Lubaŋa kikome. I kare ma amiyo gucamo cam guyeŋ adada, gutimo abor, dok guwoto kacel gucito i odi pa malaya.
Jeremia 5:8 Gipitogi guyeŋ maber macalo twon aguragura ma mito tigo, kun ŋat acel acel kok pi dako pa lawote.
Jeremia 5:9 Pe abiketo can i komgi pi lok magi? man Rwot ma openyo; dok bene pe abiculo kwor i kom rok macalo man?
Jeremia 5:10 “Kat icit i potone ki i kin olok ci ilwer, ento pe ityekgi woko liweŋ; Lwer jaŋe woko, pien gin pe gubedo pa Rwot.
Jeremia 5:11 Pien jo me ot pa Icrael ki jo me ot pa Juda pe gubedo ki gen mo wacel i koma, man Rwot ma owaco.
Jeremia 5:12 Gubedo ka loko lok goba goba i kom Rwot, kun giwacci, ‘En pe bitimo gin mo; gin marac benepe bipoto i komwa; pe gibilweny i komwa ki pala lucwan, kadi ki kec bene pe bipoto i lobowa.
Jeremia 5:13 Lunebi gibilokke gidoko yamo; ma lok pa Lubaŋa pe i igi. Meno gin ma bitimme i komgi!’ ”
Jeremia 5:14 Pi meno Rwot Lubaŋa me mony owaco kuman ni, “Pien doŋ guloko lok man, nen, atye ka loko lokka ma tye i dogi-ni wek odok mac, ki lwak man aloko gidoko yen, ci mac biwaŋogi woko.
Jeremia 5:15 Nen, abikelo rok mo ma a ki ka mabor i komwu, wun jo me ot pa Icrael, man Rwot ma owaco. Rokke rok matek, dok rokke rok macon, rok ma wun pe wuŋeyo loko lebgi, dok bene pe wuromo niaŋ gin ma giwaco.
Jeremia 5:16 Aterogi ducu neko dano woko. Gin ducu gicogi oteka keken.
Jeremia 5:17 Gibicamo kal ma wukayo ki camwu mukene woko liweŋ; gibicamo awobewu ki anyirawu woko; gibicamo dyegiwu ki romiwu kadi wa dyaŋiwu woko; gibicamo olokwu ki odurowu. Gaŋiwu ducu ma girumogi ki cel gogo ma wugeno-ni gibijwero wo ko ki pala licwan.”
Jeremia 5:18 Rwot owacci “Ento kadi wa I kare meno pe abityekowu woko liweŋ.
Jeremia 5:19 Ka ce lutuwu gibiwacci, ‘Piŋo Rwot Lubaŋawa otimo gin magi i komwa?’ in ibiwaco botgi ni, ‘Kit macalo wubwota woko kun wubedo ka tiyo bot lubaŋa pa lurok i lobowu, kit meno wubitiyo bene bot lurok i lobo ma pe mewu.’ ”
Jeremia 5:20 Tuc lok man i ot pa Yakobo, tit pire i lobo Juda ni,
Jeremia 5:21 “Wuwiny lok man, wun lumiŋ ki jo ma wiwu odiŋ, ma waŋwu tye, ento pe wuneno, ma itwu tye, ento pe wuwinyo.
Jeremia 5:22 Pe wulwora? Man Rwot ma owaco. Komwu bene pe myel i nyi ma? Aketo kweyo obedo waŋ apokki pi nam, apokki ma ri nakanaka ma en pe twero kato ki iye; kadi bed biamwonyi me nam twagge, pe bibalo woko, kadi piine mor, pe biromo kato ki i wiye.
Jeremia 5:23 Ento lwak man gin jo ma ŋutgi tek dok lujemo ki i cwinygi; ci gulokke guŋak, gucito gigi, guweka woko.
Jeremia 5:24 Pe giwaco ki i cwinygi ni, ‘Myero walworu Rwot Lubaŋawa, ma miyo kot i karene, kot me oro ki kot me poto kot, dok ma gwoko piwa lwak kare ma giciko me kac.’
Jeremia 5:25 Balwu ma wutimo doŋ oryemo jami magi woko, balwu ogenowu noŋo jami magi mabeco.
Jeremia 5:26 Pien jo maraco gitye i kin jona; gibedo ka kiyo piny calo ludwar winyo. Giciko owicgi; ci gimako dano.
Jeremia 5:27 Odigi opoŋ ki lok roro, calo aduku ma opoŋ ki winyo; pi meno doŋ gudoko jo madito dok bene gulony,
Jeremia 5:28 gucwe dok komgi nen liyu mada. Gitimo ballataya ma ka gikke pe; pe giŋolo kop atir, pe gikonyo litino kic wek gubed maber, dok bene pe gipido lok pa jo ma piny obwoyogi kakare.”
Jeremia 5:29 Rwot owacci, “Pe abiketo can i komgi pi lok magi? Dok bene pe abiculo kwor i kom rok macalo man?”
Jeremia 5:30 Man ginaura mada ma miyo lworo ma doŋ otimme i lobo:
Jeremia 5:31 lunebi gitito lok goba goba, ki ajwagi bene gitye ka tiyo gin ma igi mito; jona gimaro kit tim macalo meno. Ento gibitimme niŋniŋ ka agikkine doŋ oo?
Jeremia 6:1 Wun jo pa Benjamin, wuriŋ woko wular komwu! Wua woko ki i Jerucalem! Wukut tum okoki i Tekoa, ci wutiŋ bendera malo i Betakerem, pien gin marac tye ka bino a ki yo tuŋ acam, ma bityeko lobo woko liweŋ.
Jeremia 6:2 Wun jo Cion, wubedo calo olet maber pi ka cam pa dyaŋ.
Jeremia 6:3 Doŋ lukwat ki romigi ki dyegigi gibibino ka lweny i kome; ci giguro kemagi girume kwede woko dyere; gibikwayo lim makwogi kenyo, kun dano acel acel kwanyo kabedo ma en oyero.
Jeremia 6:4 Gibiwacci, “Yub lweny doŋ ikome! Wuyubbe doŋ wabicito walwenyo i kome cwiny dyeceŋ!” Ci dok gibiwacci, “Can i wiwa, pien ceŋ doŋ oleŋo woko cok poto, pien tipo ma umo piny otyeno-ni doŋ olyanne woko mabor!”
Jeremia 6:5 “Wuyubbe, wek wacitu walwenyu i kome dyewor, wek wabalu kabedone woko!”
Jeremia 6:6 Pien Rwot me mony owaco kuman ni, “Wutoŋ yadine-gu woko ducu piny; wutor cel lobo wurum ki Jerucalem woko. Man en aye gaŋ ma myero giket can i kome; pien jo ma iye gibedo ka uno dano.
Jeremia 6:7 Kit macalo waŋ it gwoko piine bedo maleŋ, Jerucalem bene kit meno tye ka gwoko tim maraco. Awinyo tim bwami ki nek i dye gaŋ; aneno two ki waŋ bur keken iye.
Jeremia 6:8 Wuwek lok man obed calo lok ma acikowu kwede, wun jo Jerucalem, wek pe aa awekwu woko; wek bene pe awek gaŋwu odok o bur, lobo ka ma dano mo pe bedo iye.”
Jeremia 6:9 Rwot me mony owacci, “Gibikwanyo jo Icrael woko liweŋ calo gipwono nyig olok ki i jaŋe, ŋat mo ma bidoŋ pe. Pi meno myero ilar jo ma itwero larogi, calo lapur ma beko nyig olokke.”
Jeremia 6:10 Agamo ni, “Abiloko bot aŋa wek acikgi, wek guwiny lokka? Nen, gudiŋo itgi woko, pe gitwero winyo loko Nen, gukwero winyo pwonnyi, gicayo lokki ma iloko-gu acaya, ai Rwot, pe giketo iye cwinygi.
Jeremia 6:11 Pi meno doŋ aol woko ki akemo pa Rwot; doŋ aol woko ki tiŋone. “To akemoni i kom litino ma gitye i dye yo, ki i kom awobe ma gucokke kacel bene. Co kacel ki mon gibikwanyogi giterogi woko, jo muteggi ki jo muti.
Jeremia 6:12 Gibimiyo odigi woko bot jo mukene, pottigi kacel ki mongi; pien abiketo can i kom jo ma gibedo i lobo-ni,” man Rwot ma owaco.
Jeremia 6:13 “Cakke i kom jo matino o kwede wa i kom jo madito dano acel acel owor woko pi lim pi noŋo magoba i yo ma pe atir; cakke i kom lunebi o kwede wa i kom ajwagi, gin ducu gitiyo ki goba keken ma pe gigenne,
Jeremia 6:14 Gibedo ka tuko ki waŋ bur pa jona atuka ma pe gicano woko liweŋ, kun giwacci, ‘Kuc, kuc,’ ma noŋo kun kuc mo pe.
Jeremia 6:15 Tika yam lewic omakogi i kare ma gutiyo gin me kwer? Pe gire, lewic mo pe omakogi wacel; pe gumiyo waŋgi omyeno wacel ki lewic. Pi meno gin gibipoto calo jo mukene ma doŋ gibipoto-ni i kare ma abiketo can i komgi gibitum woko ducu.” Man Rwot ma owaco.
Jeremia 6:16 Rwot owaco bot jone kuman ni “Wucuŋ ka ma yo oŋolle iye wek wunen, dok wupeny bene pi yo me kare macon, ka ma yo maber tye iye, wun bene wucak wot wulubi, wek wunoŋ yweyo ki kuc i cwinywu. Ento gin giwacci, ‘Wan pe wabilubo yone kadi ki acel.’
Jeremia 6:17 Aketo lukur-piny me kurowu kun awacci, ‘Wuwiny koko tum!’ Ento gin guwacci, ‘Pe wabiwinyone kadi matidi mo.’
Jeremia 6:18 Pi meno wuwiny wun lwak me rok ducu, dok wuŋe gin ma bipoto i komgi, wun lurok ma wucokke kany.
Jeremia 6:19 Winy ba, in lobo, nen, atye ka kelo gin marac wek opot i kom lwak man, winyo lokka, dok bene gukwero lubo cikka woko.
Jeremia 6:20 Piŋo gikelo odok luban bota ki i lobo Ceba, nyo lum malim ma ŋwece kur ki i lobo ma tye ka mabor? Gitum awaŋawu ducu pe abigamo kadi wa gityerwu-gu ducu pe yomo cwinya.
Jeremia 6:21 Pi meno Rwot owaco kuman ni ‘Abicibo gin mayoko dano i waŋayo pa lwak man, ma ka gibiwot giyokke kwede matek; wego kacel ki litino, luwotgi kacel ki luremgi ducu gibito.’ ” Mony ma oa ki yo tuŋ acam
Jeremia 6:22 Rwot owaco kuman ni “Nen, lwak me lok mo-ni tye ka bino kun gia ki i lobo ma yo tuŋ acam, rok matek ma tye ka mabor mada tye ka yubbe pilweny.
Jeremia 6:23 Doŋ gumako, atumgi ki toŋigi woko likiŋ, giger adada, pe gitye ki ki ca mo wacel; woogi winnye calo nam ma tye ka mor. Giriŋo ki aguragura, ma gurye woko, calo jo ma doŋ kuro lweny akura, i komwu wun jo Cion!”
Jeremia 6:24 Doŋ watyeko winyo lok ma gikelo botwa pire, ciŋwa ducu okwe woko ma doŋ pe timo gin mo; remcwiny madwoŋ dok oketo komwa wokoducu, calo arem pa dako ma, tye ka rem ki nywal.
Jeremia 6:25 Pe wukatwokowucit i dye bar, pe bene wuwot i yo; pien lukworwu gitye ki pala lucwan, i kabedo ducu inoŋo tye gin ma kelo lworo i kom dano.
Jeremia 6:26 Wun jona, wutwe boŋo cola i pyerwu, dok bene wubed ka ŋenne i buru. Wukok kit macalo onoŋo wutwero kok kwede pi latin acel keken ka oto, wukok ki keccwiny kun pig waŋwu cwer adada; pien ŋat ma bino ka tyekowa-ni bibino oyotoyot poto woko i komwa.
Jeremia 6:27 “Atyeko keti i kin jona me bedo ŋat ma niyogi dok ma temogi; temgi wek iŋe dok inoŋ kit ma gibedo kwede.
Jeremia 6:28 Gin ducu jo ma lujemo ima ŋutgi nwaŋ, ma giwoto ki lok kwot keken i kabedo ducu; gubedo matek calo mola ki nyonyo, giri ducu lutim bal keken.
Jeremia 6:29 Lutet gubuko mac olyetti okur adada ma mwoc matek, mac doŋ olenyo cet nyonyo woko, doŋ ŋat ma tye ka liyone yelle noŋo, pien jo maraco pe gikwanyogi giterogi woko cen.
Jeremia 6:30 Gibilwoŋogi ni cet ryal ma gikwero, pien Rwot doŋ otyeko kwerogi woko.”
Jeremia 7:1 Lok pa Rwot obino bot Jeremia ma wacci,
Jeremia 7:2 “Cuŋ i doggola me ot pa Rwot, ci itit lok man kunnu, kun iwacci, Wuwiny lok pa Rwot, wun jo ducu ma wudonyo ki i doggola magi kun wucito ka woro Rwot.
Jeremia 7:3 Rwot me mony, ma Lubaŋa pa Icrael, owaco kuman ni, Wuyub kitwu kacel ki tim mewu ducu, ci abiweko wubedo i kabedo man.
Jeremia 7:4 Pe wubed ka geno lwak lok magi me bwola-gu, ni, ‘Man ot pa Rwot, ot pa Rwot, ot pa Rwot.’
Jeremia 7:5 “Pien ka ce wuyubo kitwu ki timwu ducu adada, ka ce wuŋolo kop ma atir i kinwu kekenwu,
Jeremia 7:6 ka ce pe wuuno labedo mo, litino kic nyo mon to, dok bene pe wuneko dano ma pe ki bal i kabedo man, ma pe wuworo lubaŋa mukene ma miyo wupoto i can,
Jeremia 7:7 ci abimiyo wubedo i kabedo man, i lobo ma yam amiyo bot kwarowu i kare macon me bedo megi matwal-li.
Jeremia 7:8 “Nen, wuketo genwu i lok me bwola ma pe konyo-gu.
Jeremia 7:9 Pud wukwalo kwo, pud wuneko dano, wutimo abor, wukwoŋo kwoŋ gobagoba, pud wuwaŋo odok eceta bot Baal, dok bene wuworo lubaŋa mogo ma yam pe onoŋo koŋ wuŋeyo.
Jeremia 7:10 Wubedo ka timo gin ma iya dagi, dok bene wubino wucuŋ kwede i nyima i ot man, ma gilwoŋo ki nyiŋa, kun wuwacci, ‘Doŋ gilarowa woko!’ Ento pud dok wumedde ki timo gin magi me kwer i koma!
Jeremia 7:11 Wutamo ni oda ma gilwoŋo ki nyiŋa-ni odoko boro pa luyak ki botwu? Nen, an kikoma aye doŋ atyeko nenone, man Rwot ma owaco.
Jeremia 7:12 Kombeddi doŋ wucit i Cilo i kabedona macon, ka ma yam aketo nyiŋa obedo iye mukwoŋo, wek wunen gin ma atiyo iye pi gin maraco ma jona Icrael gutimo.
Jeremia 7:13 Wun doŋ wutimo gin magi ducu ma akwanogi-ni, Kadi bed abedo ka wacciwu lok teretere, ento wun wukwero winyone woko, dok bene i kare ma alwoŋowu, wun pe wugamo doga, man Rwot ma owaco.
Jeremia 7:14 Pi meno abitimo gin ma atimo i Cilo i kom oda ma gilwoŋo ki nyina ma wuketo iye genwu-ni. Abitiyo gin ma rom kit meno i kabedo man ma yam amiyo botwu ki bot kwarowu, kit macalo nene atiyo i Cilo.
Jeremia 7:15 Abiryemowu woko ducu ki i nyima, kit macalo aryemo kwede lutuwu ma likwayo pa Epraim.
Jeremia 7:16 “Doŋ in Jeremia, pe myero ileg pi lwak man, pe itiŋ dwani ka koko nyo ka lega pigi; pe ibak dogi bota pigi bene, pien pe abiwinyo lokki kadi ki acel.
Jeremia 7:17 Pe ineno gin ma gitye ka tiyone i gaŋi me Juda ducu ki i dye yo me Jerucalem?
Jeremia 7:18 Litino gicoko yen, wegigi gimoko mac, ki mon ginywaŋo moko me tedo mugati pi daker me polo; dok bene gionyo gityer amata-gu bot lwak lubaŋa, pi ŋeto cwinya wek kiniga omaka.
Jeremia 7:19 Man an aye ma gitye ka ŋeto cwinya-ni? Man Rwot ma owaco. Pe gitye ka kelo can i komgi kengi, ma miyo lewic makogi?
Jeremia 7:20 Mumiyo Rwot Lubaŋa owaco kuman ni, nen, abitoyo kinigana ki akemona woko i kom kabedo man, i kom dano ki i kom lee, i kom yadi ma i tim-gu ki ginapita ducu mucek i poto; macce biwaŋ adada ma pe gitwero nekone.”
Jeremia 7:21 Rwot me mony ma en Lubaŋa me Icrael owaco kuman ni, “Wurib gitum awaŋawu i kom gitum mukene-gu, dok wucam riŋone.
Jeremia 7:22 Pien i kare ma akwanyo kwarowu akelogi woko ki i lobo Ejipt, pe acikogi pi lok i kom gitum awaŋa ki gitum mukene-gu.
Jeremia 7:23 Ento acikogi ni myero guwiny lokka, wek abed Lubaŋagi, dok wek gin gubed jona. Dok acikogi me lubo kit ma acikogi me bedo kwede, wek gubed ma jami ducu woto maber botgi.
Jeremia 7:24 Ento gin pe gulubo cikka, dok bene pe guciko itgi ka winyo lokka, ento gubedo ka lubo tamgi kengi ki nwaŋ cwinygi ma opoŋ ki gin marac, ci gujer gudok woko cen ki ŋegi ma pe gumedde guwoto anyim.
Jeremia 7:25 Cakke i kare ma kwarowu gua kwede woko ki i lobo Ejipt o kwede wa ka onyoo, abedo ka cwalo botgi luticca ma gin lunebi teretere, nino ki nino;
Jeremia 7:26 ento gin pe guwinyo lokka, pe guciko itgi bene me winyone, ento gujiŋo ŋutgi odoko tek. Gutimo gin marac adad a ma okato gin ma yam kwarogi otimo-gu woko.
Jeremia 7:27 “Kit meno, Jeremia, ibiloko lok magi ducu botgi, ento gin pe gibiwinyo lokki. Ibilwoŋogi bene, ento pe gibigamo dogi.
Jeremia 7:28 Ci ibiwaco botgi ni, ‘Man aye rok ma pe nene jone gulubo lok pa Rwot Lubaŋagi, pe bene guye lok me pwony; lok ada doŋ otyeko rwenyo woko liweŋ, pe doŋ giloko pire matwal.
Jeremia 7:29 Wulyel yer wiwu ci wubol yerre woko; wucak wo ki koko i kabedo ma odoŋ nono ma i wi godi, pien Rwot doŋ otyeko kwero dok obwoto jo me yalwak man ma akemo omake i komgi-ni.’
Jeremia 7:30 “Jo Juda doŋ gutimo gin marac i nyima. Guketo cal jogigi ma en gin me kwer ki tuŋ bota-ni i ot ma gilwoŋo ki nyiŋa, me balone woko. Man Rwot ma owaco.
Jeremia 7:31 Guyubo waŋ jok i nota pa wod pa Kinom ma gilwoŋo ni Topet, ka ma gitwero waŋo iye awobegi ki anyiragi ki mac. Pe yam acikogi ni gutim kit meno, dok bene pe abedo ka tamo lok macalo meno wacel.
Jeremia 7:32 Pi meno, nen, kare tye ka bino ma pe dok gibilwoŋo ni Topet, nyo nota pa wod pa Kinom. Gibilwoŋo ni nota me Nek: pien gibiyiko dano i Topet, pien kabedo mo pe tye ka mukene kadi ki acel.
Jeremia 7:33 Doŋ kom jo magi ma guto-ni bidoko cam pa winyo ki pa lee me tim; ŋat mo pe ma biryemogi woko.
Jeremia 7:34 Lobo bidoko tim aroo, doŋ i gaŋi me Juda ki i dye gudo me Jerucalem abijuko woo me yomcwiny ma dano gitye kwede, kadi wa dwan lanyom ki dwan nyako ger bene.
Jeremia 8:1 “I kare meno cogo pa luker me Juda, cogo pa rwodine, cogo pa ajwagi, cogo pa lunebi, ki cogo pa jo ducu ma gibedo i Jerucalem gibikwanyo giwoto woko ka maleŋ ki i lyelgi. Man Rwot ma owaco.
Jeremia 8:2 Ci gibimoyogi woko i nyim ceŋ ki dwe ki i nyim lakalatwe me polo, ma yam gumarogi kun gitiyo botgi-ni, ma yam gubedo ka lubo korgi, ma yam guyenyo tam ki botgi ka guworo-ni, Pe gibicokogi kacel kadi ki yikogi, gibibedo calo cet dyaŋ muket ata i nom.
Jeremia 8:3 Jo ducu me rok man marac ma gubwot, ma gibedo i kabedo ka ma yam aryemogi gucito iye, gibimito ni twara kono gito woko loyo ma gibedo kwo. Man lok ma Rwot me mony aye owaco.
Jeremia 8:4 “Ibiwaco botgi ni, Rwot owaco kuman ni, Ka dano gupoto piny, pe dok gia malo? Ka ce ŋat mo oŋak woko, ci en pe lokke dwogo cen?
Jeremia 8:5 Piŋo rok man kono guŋak woko ma gitye ka medde ameda ki weko yona? Gimoko woko likiŋ i lok me bwola, gikwero lokke woko me dwogo cen.
Jeremia 8:6 Abedo ka tero ita ka winyo lokgi, ento gin pe guloko lok ma tye atir; dano ma ŋut i gin maraco ma en otimo pe, kun wacci, ‘Onoŋo atimo gin aŋo?’ Ŋat acel acel gire woto kit ma iye mito, calo aguragura ma tye ka ŋwec laro lweny.
Jeremia 8:7 Kadi winyo acebe ma bedo malo i polo bene ŋeyo karene me dwogo cen; ki akuri, lakalagwec ki ogoro gigwoko karegi me binogi; ento jona gikwiya cik ducu ma Rwot yam omiyo.
Jeremia 8:8 “Wutwero waco niŋniŋ ni, ‘Wan waryek, cik pa Rwot bene tye botwa’? Nen doŋ lupwony-cik ma pe gigenne gutyeko loko cik woko ki cocgi, guloko odoko lok goba.
Jeremia 8:9 Lewic bimako luryeko, cwinygi biballe ci gimakogi woko. Nen, gutyeko kwero lok pa Rwot; kit ryeko aŋo ma dok gitye kwede?
Jeremia 8:10 Pi meno abimiyo mongi woko bot co mukene, ki pottigi bot jo ma otayogi ki lweny, pien cakke ki i kom jo matino o kwede wa i kom jo madito dano acel acel owor woko i noŋo magoba i yo ma pe atir; cakke ki i kom lunebi o kwede wa i kom ajwagi gin ducu gitiyo ki goba keken ma pe gigenne.
Jeremia 8:11 Gibedo ka tuko ki waŋ bur pa jona atuka ma pe gicano woko liweŋ, kun giwacci, ‘Kuc, kuc,’ ma noŋo kun kuc mo pe.
Jeremia 8:12 Tika yam lewic omakogi i kare ma gutiyo gin me kwer? Pe gire, lewic mo pe omakogi wacel; pe gumiyo waŋgi omyeno wacel ki lewic. Pi meno gin bene gibipoto calo jo mukene ma gibipoto; kare ma abiketo can i komgi gibitum woko ducu.” Man Rwot ma owaco.
Jeremia 8:13 “I kare ma onoŋo myero acokgi, man Rwot ma owaco, nyig olok pe tye i wi yat olok, ki nyig oduro bene pe i wi yat oduro; pote-gu bene ducu otwo woko, ki gin ma yam amiyogi-ni bene doŋ otyeko kato woko ki botgi.”
Jeremia 8:14 Piŋo pud dok wabedo mot? Wugurre kacel wek wacitu i gaŋi ma girumo ki cel gogo wek wacitoyu kunnu; pien Rwot Lubaŋawa doŋ oketo can i komwa ni wato, omiyowa bene pii ma tye iye kwir marac wamato, pien onoŋo doŋ watimo bal i kom Rwot.
Jeremia 8:15 Wabedo ka yenyo kuc, ento gin mo maber ma wano ŋo pe, i kare ma onoŋo myero wacaŋ iye, wanoŋo gin ma kelo lworo keken.
Jeremia 8:16 “Yweyo me kiniga pa aguragura pa lukworwa winnye wa i Dan; ka twoni aguraguragi okok ci lobo ducu yeŋŋe. Gubino ka balo lobowa woko kacel ki jami ducu ma tye iye, pi jwero gaŋwa woko kacel ki jo ma gibedo iye.
Jeremia 8:17 Pien nen, atye ka cwalo twol ikinwu, twol uyu ma kwirre rac ma pe gitwero baŋone ki yat, ci gibikayowu malit,” man Rwot ma owaco. Cwerariny pa Jeremia pi lutugi
Jeremia 8:18 Can ma atye kwede doŋ dit ma pe romo caŋ, atye ki two madit me cwercwiny mada i cwinya.
Jeremia 8:19 Koŋ iwiny, koko pa jona orumo i lobo woko ducu, kun gikok ni, “Rwot mono pe i Cion? Kabakane mono doŋ pe iye?” Rwot ma kabakagi ogamo ni, “Piŋo kono wuŋeto cwinya ki cal jogiwu, wumiyo kiniga omaka ki lubaŋa pa lurok mogo ma pe gikonyo-gu?”
Jeremia 8:20 Dano gikok ni, “Kare me kac doŋ okato woko, ki kare me oro bene dog ogik, ento pud pe gilarowa.”
Jeremia 8:21 Cwinya rem calo bur odet iye pien jona doŋ giketo bur woko i komgi, akumo pi can, ma cwercwiny doŋ obwoyo koma woko.
Jeremia 8:22 Yat me caŋo dano doŋ pe i Gilead bo? Daktar kono pe kunnu? Piŋo kono pe gicano jona?
Jeremia 9:1 Ka twerre onoŋo myero wiya obed waŋ it me pii, ki waŋa noŋo myero obed. Waŋ it ma gunnye ki pig waŋ, wek omiya abed ka kok dyeceŋ ki dyewor benebene pi jona ma dog ginekogi woko-ni.
Jeremia 9:2 Onoŋo amito ni kono nene kabedo mo obed tye ma abedo iye macalo ka gony pa luwot i tim aroo, kono aweko jona ci acito woko ka mabor kwedgi! Gin ducu lutim abor, gin ducu lutim tim aranyi.
Jeremia 9:3 Gin kare ducu guyubbe woko me loko lok goba; bedo laboŋo gen doŋ oloyo lobo woko ma kaka tim me ada. Rwot owacci, “Sona gitimo gin marac teretere, dok bene pe giŋeya.”
Jeremia 9:4 Dano acel acel myero ogwokke i kom lawote, ki bene pe myero ogen ominne: pien omego acel acel obedo labwola calo Yakobo, dok dano acel acel bene kwoto lawote.
Jeremia 9:5 Ŋat acel acel bwolo lawote, dano mo ma loko ada pe; doŋ gutyekopwonyo Lebgi woko me loko lok goba, gitimo bal giyelle iye adada ma pe giromo ŋut.
Jeremia 9:6 Gibedo ka uno dano teretere, dok gitimo gin me bwola teretere, gikwero woko ni pe giŋeya, man Rwot ma owaco.
Jeremia 9:7 Mumiyo Rwot me mony owaco kuman ni, “Nen, abitemogi macalo nyonyo ma giliyo. Jona doŋ gutimo gin marac, gin aŋo kono ma dok atwero tiyo kwedgi?
Jeremia 9:8 Lebgi obedo calo atero ma lake ki kwir marac; giloko lok me bwola keken. Dano acel acel loko lok mamit bot lawote, ento ki i cwinye noŋo tye ki yub me kanne wek eneke woko.
Jeremia 9:9 An pe abiketo can i komgi pi lok magi? Pe abiculo kwor i kom rok macalo man?” Man Rwot ma owaco.
Jeremia 9:10 Jeremia owacci, “Wek dog akok pi godi, dok abikok kun cwinya cwer pi olet-gu, pien doŋ gutwo woko, ŋat mo ma woto kun ŋolo ki iye doŋ pe. Koko pa dyaŋi bene pe doŋ winnye kunnu; winyo ki lee tim ducu doŋ guriŋo gurwenyo woko, doŋ gipe matwal.”
Jeremia 9:11 Rwot owacci, “Abiloko Jerucalem doko wi obur me gin ma gimuko ki iye, kabedo ma too-aye bedo iye: gaŋi me Juda ducu doŋ bidoko tim noŋo, ka ma ŋat mo pe bedo iye.”
Jeremia 9:12 Dano mene maryek ma wacci etwero niaŋ lok man? Rwot mono oloko lok magi bot aŋa, ni wek otit lokke? Piŋo lobo doŋ oballe woko odoko wi obur calo tim ma iye odoŋ nono, ma dano mo pe wok kato ki iye?
Jeremia 9:13 Rwot owacci, “Man otimme pien jona gubwoto cikka ma nene amiyo botgi-ni, dok bene pe guwinyo lokka, pe gubedo kun gilubo cikka.
Jeremia 9:14 Ento ma ka timo meno gumiyo ŋutgi obedo nwaŋ, gubedo ka woro jogi Baal mapatpat, kit macalo kwarogi opwonyogi kwede.
Jeremia 9:15 Pi meno Rwot me mony, ma en Lubaŋa pa Icrael, owaco kuman ni, Nen, abimiyo jo magi gimato yat roka, dok bene abimiyo gimato pii ma giketo iye kwir.
Jeremia 9:16 Abikeyogi woko i kin lurok ma gin kikomgi pe giŋeyo, kadi wa kwarogi bene yam pe guŋeyo; abicwalo dul mony lubo korgi ki pala lucwan nio waŋ ma atyekogi woko liweŋ.”
Jeremia 9:17 Rwot me mony owaco kuman, ni, “Koŋ wutam lok, ci wulwoŋ monma giŋeyo wer koko-gu gubin; wucwal lok wulwoŋ mon makwiri gubin;
Jeremia 9:18 wek gurune gubin oyotoyot ci guwo ki koko i komwa, wek pig waŋwa omo locit piny lipyaa, ma del waŋwa bene odyak woko ki pii.
Jeremia 9:19 Koŋ wuwiny dwan me koko ma a ki i Cion, ‘Doŋ watum woko do! Lewic doŋ omakowa woko marac, pien doŋ waa woko ki i lobowa, pien aaniwa doŋ gijwero woko licwic.’ ”
Jeremia 9:20 Jeremia owacci, “Wun mon, wuwiny doŋ lok ma Rwot owaco, wucik itwu wek wuwiny lok ma oa ki i doge. Wupwony anyirawu ki koko, Ŋat acel acel opwony lawote ki wer lyel.
Jeremia 9:21 To doŋ obino woko i komwa ki i waŋ dirica, ci odonyo woko i gaŋ kalwa ducu, oneko litino woko ducu ki i dye yo ki awobe-gu ki i dye bar.
Jeremia 9:22 Kom jo muto gibikeyo woko ata gikeyo woko macalo odur cet dyaŋ muket ata i olet, calo kal ma lukac gukayo guweko odoŋ i poto, ma ŋat mo doŋ pe ma bicoko tero i gaŋ. Man aye gin ma Rwot owacca ni atiti.” Ŋeyo Lubaŋa aye deyo ma dano tye kwede
Jeremia 9:23 Rwot owacca kuman ni, “Dano maryek myero pe onyatte ki ryekone-ni, kadi ki dano matek bene pe myero onyatte ki tekone, ki dano mulony bene pe myero onyatte ki lonyone.
Jeremia 9:24 Ento ka ŋat mo mito nyatte, myero onyatte ni eniaŋ dok eneyo an, ni an a Rwot ma atye ka tiyo gin ma nyuto mar ma pe lokke, anyuto bene ŋolo kop atir ki bedo ki kit ma atir i lobo. Magi gin aye jami ma cwinya mito. Man Rwot ma owaco.”
Jeremia 9:25 Rwot owacci, “Nen nino tye ka bino, en aye kare ma abiketo iye can i kom jo ma gilirogi ki i del komgi ki woko ento pe ki i cwinygi.
Jeremia 9:26 Abiketo can i kom Jo Ejipt, jo Juda, jo Edom, jo Ammon, jo Moab ki jo ducu ma gibedo i tim aroo ma ginyaro yer wigi woko doŋ macego; rok magi ducu pe gulirre ki i cwinygi, ki jo me ot pa Icrael bene pe gulirre ki i cwinygi.”
Jeremia 10:1 Wun jo Icrael wuwiny lok ma Lubaŋa tye ka lokone botwu.
Jeremia 10:2 Rwot owaco kuman ni, “Pe wupwony kit pa lurok, dok cwinywu bene pe myero oballe ka wuneno lanyut mo tye i polo, kadi bed rok mukene-gu cwinygi oballe woko pire.
Jeremia 10:3 Pien kit pa lurok obedo gin me bwolo, pe ada. Gitoŋo yat gireto woko piny i buŋa, ci lapac payo woko maber ki koyone nyo ki jami mukene me pac.
Jeremia 10:4 Dano gidero kome woko ki ryal nyojabu; gikwanyo nyono giguro ki cumari iye wek ocun matek likiŋ pe opot woko piny.
Jeremia 10:5 Cal lubaŋagi-nu obedo calo wir yat ma gicibo ocun i poto okwer pi ryemo winyo, pe bene gitwero lok; gitiŋogi mege atiŋa, pien pe giwoto. Pe ilworgi, pe gitwero timo gin mo marac i komi, dok bene pe gitye ki twero mo me timo gin mo maber.”
Jeremia 10:6 Pe tye lubaŋa mo macalo in, ai Rwot; in idit, dok nyiŋi bene dit ki tek.
Jeremia 10:7 Aŋa mono ma pe myero olwori, in kabaka ma loyo rok ducu? Man aye kiti, myero dano gulwori. Pe tye ŋat mo macalo in i kin luryeko ducu me rok mapatpat, kadi ki i te kergi ducu.
Jeremia 10:8 Danogi ducu ma luryeko gubedo jo ma lumiŋ dok wigi bene odiŋ. En bao ma giyubo ni cal lubaŋa-ni tika pwonyogi ki gin mo?
Jeremia 10:9 Cal lubaŋagi gidero kome woko ki ryal ma gidino woko ma gikelo ki i Tarcic, ki jabu ma gikelo ki i Upaj, Gin ducu gubedo tic pa lupac ki dok bene tic ma latet jabu otiyo ki ciŋe: ginarukagi obedo makwar ki dok lamar lamar; gin ducu gubedo tic ma jo ma kwiri aye gutiyo.
Jeremia 10:10 Ento Rwot aye Lubaŋa me ada, en Lubaŋa makwo, dok bene en Kabaka ma bedo nakanaka. Ka inen, ce akemo omake ci lobo yeŋŋe, rok ducu pe twero ciro kinigane.
Jeremia 10:11 Ibiwaco botgi kit man ni, “Lubaŋa mogo-gu ma pe guketo polo ki lobo-ni gibijwerogi woko. Pe doŋ gibibedo tye i kabedo mo i wi lobo ki i te polo.” Wer me pako Lubaŋa
Jeremia 10:12 Rwot oketo lobo ki twerone, dok ocibo lobo ocuŋ matek pi ryekone, ki pi niaŋ matut ma en tye kwede omiyo oyaro polo woko.
Jeremia 10:13 I kare ma dwane mor, ci pii twagge matek ki i polo, dok miyo lupu duny kun a ki i agikki lobo. En miyo lutkot wil ka kot cwer, dok bene miyo yamo kodo kun a ki i ot kano jamine.
Jeremia 10:14 Dano ducu bedo lumiŋ dok bene ma wigi odiŋ; lewic mako latet jabu pi cal jokke ma en otiyo; pien cal jogine-gu ducu pe lubaŋa me ada, dok bene pe gitye ki kit kwo mo i igi.
Jeremia 10:15 Konygi pe, gitiyogi mere me acaya keken; i kare ma Rwot bibino ka keto can i komgi gibito gitum woko.
Jeremia 10:16 Lubaŋa pa Yakobo pe obedo calo cal jogi magi; pien en aye ŋat ma oketo jami ducu, dok bene en oyero jo Icrael wek gubed jone kikome, Nyiŋe gilwoŋo ni Rwot me mony.
Jeremia 10:17 Wun jo Jerucalem ma mony doŋ orumowu woko-ni, wutiŋ yecwu woko ki i ŋom,
Jeremia 10:18 pien kombeddi doŋ Rwot biryemowu woko ki i lobo-ni; en biŋinyowu waŋ ma wuwinyo litte. Man Rwot ma owaco.
Jeremia 10:19 Jo Jerucalem gikok ni, “Giketo ret woko i komwa marac kuman! Waŋ burwa tye marac mada ma pe bicaŋ. Yam watamo ni man en aye gin ma watwero ciro, kara pe!
Jeremia 10:20 Kemawa doŋ gibalo woko, ki tol ducu ma onoŋo gitweyogi kwede gicodo woko; litinowa doŋ guwekowa, gin ducu doŋ gipe. Ŋat mo pe ma odoŋ ma myero ogur kemawa odoco kakare; pe tye ŋat mo ma myero otwe boŋo kicika megi malo.”
Jeremia 10:21 Jeremia ogamo ni, “Lutel doŋ gudoko lumiŋ; pe gipenyo Rwot wek otelgi. Meno aye gin mumiyo yam pe gubedo maber; lwakgi ducu doŋ guket woko ata.
Jeremia 10:22 “Winy lok! Nen tye ka bino! Twon gin ma mor tye ka katti bino ki i lobo ma yo tuŋ acam, dul monnye bino me jwero gaŋi me Juda woko wek odoŋ obur, odok kabedo ka ma too bedo iye.”
Jeremia 10:23 Ai Rwot, aŋeyo ni dano pe loyo kwone kene nio i agikkine; pe tye ŋat mo ma tye ki twero me loyo kwoŋo.
Jeremia 10:24 Ai Rwot, pwony lwakwa; ento pe itimwa marac aye. Pe ipwonywa i kare ma noŋo kiniga omaki; miyo wabito woko ducu.
Jeremia 10:25 Kiniga myero omaki i kom rok ma pe giŋeyi, ki i kom lurok ma pe gilwoŋo nyiŋi-ni. Doŋ gityeko likwayo pa Yakobo woko; ci gubalo lobowa woko odoŋ obur.
Jeremia 11:1 Rwot oloko ki Jeremia, ni,
Jeremia 11:2 “Winy lok ma mako gicikke nan. Tit bot jo Juda ki jo ma gibedo Jerucalem ni,
Jeremia 11:3 an, Rwot Lubaŋa pa crael, doŋ atyeko ceno dano ma pe winyo dok ma pe lubo lok ma mako icikke man.
Jeremia 11:4 En gicikke ma yam keto ki kwarowu i kare ma akwanyogi woko ki i lobo Ejipt, en lobo ma obedo alo buk mac me teto nyonyo ma otwak me waŋogi. I kare meno awaco otgi ni guwiny lokka dok guti gin ducu ma yam acikogi ni guti. Atito otgi ni ka gulubo ci gibibedo jona kin bene abibedo Lubaŋagi.
Jeremia 11:5 Aciko botgi ni an bene abicobo kwoŋ ma am akwoŋo i nyim kwarogi kun miyo botgi lobo ma mol cak ki moo Ic, kit macalo gitye iye wa onyoo-ni.” Ci an Jeremia agamo ni, “Wek obed kumeno, Rwot.”
Jeremia 11:6 Rwot dok owacca ni, “Tit lok magi ducu i gaŋi me Juda, ki i dye yo me Jerucalem. Tit lokka kunnu, kun iwaco bot lwak ni guwiny lok ma mako gicikke man dok bene gulubi kun gitiyo.
Jeremia 11:7 I kare ma akwanyo kwarowu woko ki i lobo Ejipt, acikogi matek, kun bene abedo ka cikogi teretere, nio wa onyoo, kun awaco botgi ni gulub lokka.
Jeremia 11:8 Ento gin pe gulubo dok pe guciko itgi me winyo lokka. Ma ka timo meno, dano acel acel omedde ameda ki bedo ki nwaŋ cwiny marac. Mumiyo acobo lok me gicikke man woko ducu i komgi, ma yam acikogi ni guti, ento pe gutiyo-ni.”
Jeremia 11:9 Rwot dok owaco bota ni, “Jo Juda kacel ki jo ma bedo i Jerucalem gitye ka jemo woko i koma.
Jeremia 11:10 Gulokke gudok cen ka timo bal pa kwarogi ma gukwero winyo lokka woko-ni; gubedo ka lubo lubaŋa mukene kun giworogi bene: Jo me ot pa Icrael ki jo me ot pa Juda doŋ guturo gicikkena woko ma yam acikke kwede ki kwarogi-ni.
Jeremia 11:11 Pi meno Rwot owaco kuman ni, Nen, atye ka kelo gin marac wek aket i komgi ma pe gitwero loyo ki iye wacel. Ka gibikok bota pi kony, an pe abiwinyo kokogi.
Jeremia 11:12 I kare meno jo Juda kacel ki jo ma bedo i Jerucalem gibicito gikok bot lubaŋa ma yam gibedo ka waŋo iye gitum botgi-ni, ento lubaŋa magi pe twero larogi i kare me can.
Jeremia 11:13 Pien lubaŋawu doŋ gudoko pol ma guporo wel gaŋiwu, wun jo Juda; ki wun jo ma wubedo i Jerucalem bene doŋ wuyubo lwak keno tyer mapol ata ka ma wuwaŋo iye gitum me lewic bot jok Baal, ma rom ki wel yo ma tye i dye gaŋ me Jerucalem.
Jeremia 11:14 “Pi meno Jeremia, pe ibed ka lega, pe bene ipid kweda pi lwak man. Ka inen ce gitye i can ka gukok bota pi kony, an pe abiwinyo kokogi.”
Jeremia 11:15 Rwot owaco ni, “Jona ma amaro-ni gitye ka timo tim kipyeda. Doŋ gitye ki kit twero aŋo ma weko gibedo i oda? Gitamo ni tyero lee me gitum ki kwoŋo kwoŋ mogo ma gicikke kwede atata twero geŋo can woko me poto i komgi? Gitamo ni gitwero bwot i yo ma kit man?
Jeremia 11:16 Yam alwoŋogi ni yat jeituni ma pote olot madwoŋ, ma nyige bene nen mwonya adada; ento abiwaŋo pote woko ki mac ma yamone mor mager, dok abituro jaŋe woko ducu.
Jeremia 11:17 “An Rwot me mony ma yam apito jo Icrael ki jo Juda, macalo yat jeituni-ni, kombeddi doŋ awacci abiketo gin marac i komgi, Gukelo gigi can man i komgi pigi kengi pien gin gutimo gin marac. Guŋeto cwinya omiyo kiniga omaka pi waŋo gitum bot jok Baal.” Lok ma gipiro pi neko Jeremia,
Jeremia 11:18 Rwot omiyo aŋeyo dok aniaŋ lok ma lukworra gupiro, ki gin marac ma onoŋo gimito timo i koma.
Jeremia 11:19 Ento an abedo calo latin romo mamwol ma gitero woko ka nekone, onoŋo pe aŋeyo ni gupiro lok me timo gin marac i koma. Gubedo ka waco ni, “Watoŋu yat man waretu woko piny wa ki nyige ducu; waneke woko wek ŋat mo pe doŋ obipo i kome matwal i lobo-ni.”
Jeremia 11:20 Lacen an Jeremia alego ni, “Ai Rwot me mony, in laŋolkop ma ŋolo kop atir, dok itemo tam pa dano ki gin ma giparo ki i cwinygi. Wek anen ka iculo kwor i kom lwak man, pien an doŋ atyeko keto lokka woko ducu i ciŋi.”
Jeremia 11:21 Pi meno Rwot owaco kuman, i kom jo Anatot, ma onoŋo gimito neko Jeremia woko kun giwacce ni ka ce en omedde ki tito lok i nyiŋ Rwot ci gibineke woko.
Jeremia 11:22 Rwot me mony owaco lok i komgi ni, “Nen, abiketo can i komgi. Awobegi ducu gibinekogi woko i lweny ki pala lucwan; litinogi ducu bito woko ki kec.
Jeremia 11:23 Ŋat mo ma bidoŋ pe ka kare oromo, en kare ma doŋ amoko me keto iye can i kom jo Anatot.”
Jeremia 12:1 Ai Rwot, ka apido lokka kwedi, anoŋo ni in giri lokki tye atir. Ento myero pud dok apenyi lok ma mako ŋolo kop. Piŋo jo maraco gibedo maber dok gilony? Piŋo lutim aranyi kono gicobo tiyo gin ma cwinygi mito?
Jeremia 12:2 In aye ma yam ipitogi, mumiyo giroyo lwitgi donyo i ŋom gidoŋo ci ginyak bene. Kare ducu gin giloko lok maber i komi, ento ki i cwinygi noŋo gitye ka mabor, pe giparo piri.
Jeremia 12:3 Ento in Rwot, iŋeya, ineno gin ma atiyo, dok itemo tamma pi neno kit macalo amari kwede. Makgi ikelgi woko ki tek calo romi me aneka, kogi woko iketgi pat nio ka nino me nekogi oromo.
Jeremia 12:4 Lobowa mono bibedo mutwo pi kare ma rom mene, dok lum ducu ma i tim bitwo woko nio wa awene? Lee ki winyo gitye ka to pi tim maraco pa jo ma gibedo i lobo man, ma giwaco ni i, “In pe ineno kit ma gitye ka bedo kwede.”
Jeremia 12:5 Rwot owacci, “Jeremia, ka ce iol woko i ŋwec ma kun ipyemki dano, ci ibiŋweco ipyem ki aguragura niŋniŋ? Ka ce ipoto piny i lobo ma kuc tye iye, ci doŋ ibikwo niŋniŋ ka ibedo i kin yadi mukadde ma tye i ŋet Jordan?
Jeremia 12:6 Kadi ki omegini, ma gin jo me ot pa woru kikome, gin bene gutimo tim aranyi i komi, gin guribbe ka lweny i komi bene. Pe igengi, kadi bed giloko lok maber me larem boti.”
Jeremia 12:7 Lubaŋa owacci, “An doŋ aweko jona woko, doŋ akwero rok ma yam ayerogi-ni woko; doŋ atyeko miyo jona ma amaro-ni woko i ciŋ lukworgi.
Jeremia 12:8 Jona ma ayerogi-ni doŋ gulokke woko i koma calo labwor ma tye i buŋa; gumor ki koko matek i koma pi meno omiyo adaggi.
Jeremia 12:9 Jona ma ayerogi-ni gubedo calo tula, ma winyo wadigi lwenyo i kome i kabedo ducu. Wubin, wun lee tim; wubin wuribbe ka cam kacel.
Jeremia 12:10 Lukwat mapol doŋ gutyeko balo poto olokka woko, gunyono dul lobo ma gipokka woko piny ki tyengi, guloko dul lobona ma yomo cwinyani odoko tim ma iye odoŋ noŋo.
Jeremia 12:11 Gumiyo doŋ odoko tim ma konnye pe; odoko tim ma iye odoŋ noŋo i nyima. Lobone ducu doŋ gibalo woko odoŋ noŋo, ento ŋat mo ma paro pire pe.
Jeremia 12:12 I wi cere ducu ma tye i tim aroo, jo ma lutyek piny doŋ gubino ka yako Doŋ an Rwot atyeko cwalo lweny me tyeko lobo woko ducu; ŋat mo pe ma bitwero bedo ki kuc.
Jeremia 12:13 Jona yam gucoyo bel ento gukayo okuto, gubedo ka tiyo tic matek guolo komgi woko, ento pe gulimo iye gin mo. Lewic bimakogi pien gin ma gucoyo ducu pe pi kiniga mager pa Rwot.” Cikke pa Rwot pi jo ma bedo ka get jo Icrael
Jeremia 12:14 Rwot owaco kuman ni, “Atye ki lok mo ma myero awac bot jo ma gibedo ka ŋet jo Icrael ma doŋ gubalo lobo ma amiyo bot jona jo Icrael-li woko. Nen, abikwanyo rok man woko ki i lobogi, dok bene abilaro jo Juda akwanyogi ki i kingi.
Jeremia 12:15 I kare ma doŋ akwanyogi woko, ci kica bimaka i komgi, Abikelo rok acel acel adwoko cen i lobone dok i kabedone kikome.
Jeremia 12:16 Dok ka kare biromo, ka ce gipwonyo kit pa jona ki cwinygi ducu, ma kun gikwoŋo ki nyiŋa ni, ‘Macalo Rwot tye makwo-ni,’ macalo yam gupwonyo jona me kwoŋo ki nyiŋ jok Baal, ci miyo gin ducu doŋ gibirubbe woko ki jona ci gibibedo maber.
Jeremia 12:17 Ento ka ce tye rok mo ma pe biwinyo lokka, ci abiputo woko ki lwite ducu ci abalo woko licwic, man Rwot ma owaco.”
Jeremia 13:1 Rwot owacca kuman ni, “Cit iwil boŋo camanini me aruka i pyer, ci itwe i pyeri, ento pe ilut i pii.”
Jeremia 13:2 Ci awilo boŋo me pyer kun alubo lok ma Rwot otitta-ni, ci aruko i pyera.
Jeremia 13:3 Lok pa Rwot dok obino bota tyen me aryone ma wacci,
Jeremia 13:4 “Kwany boŋo me pyer ma nene iwilo iruko i pyeri-ni, ci ia icit i dog kulu Euprate, ci icikan woko kunnu i kin got mubar.”
Jeremia 13:5 An aa acito ci akano woko i ŋet kulu Euprate kit macalo Rwot ocika kwede.
Jeremia 13:6 I ŋe nino mapol Rwot dok owacca ni, “A malo icit wa i kulu Euprate ci ikwany boŋo me aruka ma yam aciki ni icikan kunnu-ni.”
Jeremia 13:7 Cutcut aa acito i kulu Euprate ci akwinyo ŋom, ci akwanyo boŋo aruka me pyer ki i kabedo ka ma yam onoŋo akano iye-ni. Ento anoŋo ni boŋo ca doŋ oballe woko, pe dok ber pi gin mo.
Jeremia 13:8 Lacen Rwot dok pud oloko bota aye. En oloko bota kuman ni,
Jeremia 13:9 “Man aye kit macalo abityeko kwede wakke pa Juda ki wakke madit ma Jerucalem tye kwede.
Jeremia 13:10 Lwak magi marac ma gukwero winyo lokka, ma gumiyo ŋutgi obedo nwaŋ gulubo gigi gin ma cwinygi mito, ma gubedo ki lubaŋa mukene kun gitiyo botgi, gibibedo calo boŋo pyer man ma pe doŋ ber me aruka.
Jeremia 13:11 Kit macalo boŋo me atweya i pyer moko kwede i kom dano, kumeno bene aketo jo me ot pa Icrael ki jo me ot pa Juda aridogi woko i koma matek likiŋ, wek gubed lwak ma gibikelo nyiŋ maber bota, ma gibimiyo dano gipaka dok gimiya deyo, ento gin onoŋo pe gitwero winyo lok wacel.” Man Rwot ma owaco. Lok kom agulu ma gupoŋ woko ki koŋo vino
Jeremia 13:12 Rwot owaco kuman ni, “Jeremia, in itit lok man bot jo Icrael ni, ‘Rwot Lubaŋa me mony owaco kuman ni, “Agulu acel acel bipoŋ woko ki koŋo vino.” ’ Gibiwaco botwu ni, ‘Pe wamito waŋe ni agulu acel acel bipoŋ wo ko ki koŋo vino’
Jeremia 13:13 Ci lacen in ibiwaco botgi ni, ‘Nen, abipiko jo ducu ma gibedo i lobo man ki koŋo vino ci gidoko lumero, luker ma gibedo i wi komker pa Daudi, ajwagi, lunebi kacel ki jo ducu ma gibedo i Jerucalem.
Jeremia 13:14 Abicanyo ŋat man ki lawote, wego ki litinogi kacel, man Rwot ma owaco, Pe abiparo pigi, pe abiweko gibedo kwo, kadi wa kica bene pe bimaka i komgi, wek pe atyekgi woko.’ ”
Jeremia 13:15 Wuter itwu, wuwiny; pe myero wubed ki wakke, pien Rwot doŋ otyeko loko.
Jeremia 13:16 Wumi deyo bot Rwot Lubaŋawu ma pud peya okelo colpiny, ma pud tyenwu pe ogwaŋŋe i wi godi ma piny ribiribi; ma pud peya noŋo olokke odoko mutu macol licuc, en leŋpiny ma onoŋo wutye ka genone-ni.
Jeremia 13:17 Ka ce pe wubiwinyo, ci abikok laliŋliŋ i muŋ pi wakkewu: abikok matek noŋo pig waŋa mol cito piny lipyaa, pien jo pa Rwot doŋ giterogi woko macalo opii.
Jeremia 13:18 Rwor owaco bot Jeremia ni, “Tit bot kabaka gin ki minne ni gua ki i komkergi gubin woko i kabedo mapiny, pien lalukanagi maber twatwal doŋ opoto woko piny ki i wigi.”
Jeremia 13:19 Gaŋi me Negeb ducu doŋ gilorogi woko, pe tye ŋat mo ma myero oyabgi. Jo Juda ducu doŋ giterogi woko i lobo ma pe megi, gin ducu doŋ giterogi woko i opii.
Jeremia 13:20 “Wun jo Jerucalem wunen! Lukworwu tye ka bino kun gia ki i lobo ma tye yo tun acam! Jo ma miyogi i ciŋwu ni wugwokgini gitye kwene, danowu macalo lwak romi ki dyegi ma gibeco adada-ni?
Jeremia 13:21 Ibiwaco gin aŋo ka jo ma yam in kikomi aye ipwonyogi ni wek gubed luremi, aye giketogi me loyi? Arem matek pe biketo komi woko, calo arem pa dako ma tye ka nywal?
Jeremia 13:22 Doŋ ka ce ipenyo ni piŋo gin ma kit man obino i komi, piŋo boŋo ma i pyeri bene giyeco woko, dok ginywari kwede-gu; man otimme pien onoŋo balli doŋ rac ma okato kare.
Jeremia 13:23 Laetiopia mo tika twero loko raŋi me del kome, nyo kwac bene twero kwanye raŋi ma i kome ma obedo kwicikwicini woko? Ka tye kit meno, wun ma wuniyo ki timo gin marac keken-ni, wutwero pwonnye me tiyo gin ma tye atir.
Jeremia 13:24 Abikeyowu woko calo cuŋ kal ma yamo kodo ki i tim aroo ci tero woko.
Jeremia 13:25 Man aye gin ma gipokki, dul ma doŋ atyeko pimone woko piri, man Rwot ma owaco, pien wii doŋ otyeko wil woko i koma ibedo ka geno lok goba keken.
Jeremia 13:26 An Rwot kikoma aye ma abiwalo boŋoni woko ki i pyeri aumo ki waŋi, miyo lewicci nen woko ka maleŋ.
Jeremia 13:27 Doŋ atyeko neno gin me kwer ma itimo, tim me abor ki mito tigoni, ki tim malayani marac adada, ma ibedo ka timone i wi cere i dye tim. Can i wiwu, wun jo Jerucalem! Gin man bitero kare ma rom mene ma noŋo pud peya gilonyowu wudoko leŋ?”
Jeremia 14:1 Rwot owaco bot Jeremia pi two pii ma okemo Juda woko ni,
Jeremia 14:2 “Juda tye ka kumo gaŋine bene tye ka to woko. Jo Juda ducu gibuto piny ki twon cwercwiny mo ma pe wacce; ma noŋo jo Jerucalem gitye ka kok matek adada pi kony.
Jeremia 14:3 Luditogi me awora gicwalo luticgi ka twomo pii; gicito i waŋ taŋi me pii, emo pe ginoŋo, gidwogo ki gin latwom piigi ma noŋo iye noŋo. Lewic makogi dok bene alee twodogi woko ci giumo wigi woko.
Jeremia 14:4 Pien lobo doŋ oballe woko, kit macalo kot doŋ pe obedo ka cwer i lobo-ni, lewic omako lupur mada ma noŋo cwinygi cwer ma giumo wigi auma.
Jeremia 14:5 Kadi bed wa megi til ma tye i tim bene no no gubwoto litinogi ma gunywalo woko pien lum mo ma myero gucam pe.
Jeremia 14:6 Kana me tim-gu gicuŋ i wi cere matar atara ligwek, giŋamo doggi malac me yweyo calo too; waŋgi olwal woko pien onoŋo pe tye lum mo ma myero gucam.
Jeremia 14:7 “Kadi bed ka ce balwa dotowa, ai Rwot konywa kit macalo yam iciko. Wabedo ka lokke wabwoti woko tyen mapol; watyeko bene timo bal-gu i komi.
Jeremia 14:8 In keken aye ŋat ma jo Icrael gigeno, in aye ma ilarowa i kare ma noŋo watye i can. Piŋo ibedo macalo larok i lobowa, dok macalo lawot ma yenyo kabuto?
Jeremia 14:9 Piŋo ibedo macalo dano ma wiye onyobbe woko ma pe ŋeyo gin ma myero etim, calo ŋat mo ma en oteka ma pe twero laro dano ki i mony? Ento adada in Rwot it ye kwedwa, dok waŋ bene gilwonowa ki nyiŋi; pi meno pe ibwotwa woko.”
Jeremia 14:10 Rwot owaco kuman i komjone ni, “Yam gumaro wot atata kit meno, pe gujuko tyengi ka wot; pi meno omiyo Rwot pe gamogi. Kombeddi doŋ en bipo i kom bal megi ci biketo can i komgi pi balgi.”
Jeremia 14:11 Rwot owaco bota ni, “Pe myero ilega ni an akony lwak man.
Jeremia 14:12 Kadi bed giri kec, pe abiwinyo koko ma gikok kwede bota pi kony, dok kadi bed gutyer gitum awaŋa ki gityer me moko kwoŋ, pe abigamogi; ento abinekogi atyekogi woko liweŋ ki pala lucwan, ki kec malit mupoto i lobo, wa ki two gemo- gu.”
Jeremia 14:13 Dok awacci, “Ai Rwot Lubaŋa, nen lunebi onoŋo doŋ gutyeko tito bot lwak man woko ni, ‘Pe gibinekowu ki pala lucwan, dok bene kec mo pe bipoto i lobowu, ento Rwot bimiyo botwu kuc me ada ma bedo nakanaka i kabedo man.’ “
Jeremia 14:14 Ento Rwot odokka iye owacca ni, “Lunebi gitye ka tito lok goba keken ki nyiŋa; an pe acwalogi, pe acikogi, dok bene pe bene pe aloko kwedgi. Gitye ka tito botwu ginanyuta me goba ki tyeto tyet ma konnye pe, kun gibwolo dano abwola ki tam ma gutamo pigi kengi.
Jeremia 14:15 Pi meno an Rwot awaco kuman lok i kom lunebi ma gitito lok i nyina kadi bed an aye pe acwalogi, ma giwacci, ‘Pala lucwan ki kec madit pe bibino i kom lobo man wacel,’ awaco ni, Lunebi magi gibine-kogi ki pala lucwan kacel ki kec.
Jeremia 14:16 Jo ma gin gubedo ka tito lok botgi bene gibibologi woko i dye yo me Jerucalem, ma noŋo ginekogi ki pala lucwan kacel ki kec; ŋat mo pe ma biyikogi. Man bitimme i komgi ducu, i kom mongi, litino awobegi, ki anyiragi bene, pien abimiyo gineno can pi tim maracogi.
Jeremia 14:17 “In ibiwaco botgi lok man ni, ‘Wek pig waŋa omol ocit piny I kora lipyaa dyeceŋ ki dyewor benebene; wek pig waŋa pe ojwik woko, pien jona gityeko goyogi woko ki twon bur madit adada, ma giketo ret woko i komgi marac atika.
Jeremia 14:18 Ka ce acito woko i tim, nen, anoŋo jo ma ginekogi ki pala lucwan dwoŋ ata! Dok ka ce adonyo i gaŋ, aneno lwak dano mapatpat gitye ka two ki two me kec! Pien lunebi kacel ki ajwagi giwoto kun gitiyo ticgi i lobo, kun pe gitye ki ŋec mo.’ ”
Jeremia 14:19 In doŋ mono ikwero Juda woko matwal, Rwot? Cwinyi bene doŋ ocido woko i kom Cion bo? Piŋo doŋ ipwodowa kuman ma pe doŋ waromo can? Wabedo ka
Jeremia 14:20 Ai Rwot, waŋ doŋ waŋeyo gin maraco ma wabedo ka timone, kadi wa bal pa kwarowa ducu waŋeyo, pien ada, waŋ wabalo i komi.
Jeremia 14:21 Pe cwinyi ocid woko i komwa, pi dit me nyiŋi; dok bene pe ibal woro me komkerri ma nen me deyo-ni woko. Po piwa, pe itur gicikkeni woko kwedwa.
Jeremia 14:22 Tika tye kit lubaŋa mo i kin lubaŋa me gobagoba me rok ducu ma twero miyo kot cwer? Nyo polo kono twero miyo kot mo ŋido i lobo? Pe in aye ma itiyo magi ducu, ai Rwot Lubaŋawa? Wan ducu wageno in, pien in aye ma itiyo jami magi ducu.
Jeremia 15:1 Lacen Rwot owacca ni, “Kadi bed Moses ki Camuel gubedo ka Cuŋ i nyima kun gipido kweda, an kica pe bimaka i kom lwak man wacel. Wek gua ki i nyima gucit woko.
Jeremia 15:2 Ka ce inen gupenyo ka kwene ma myero gicit iye, wuwac botgi ni an Rwot awaco botgi ni, “Jo mogo bito woko ki two gemo, meno en aye ka ma gibicito iye! Jo mukene gibito i lweny ginekogi woko ki pala lucwan, meno en aye ka ma gibicito iye! Jo mogo kec aye ma binekogi meno en aye ka ma gibicito iye! Ki jo mogo gibimakogi giterogi woko macalo opii, meno en aye ka ma gibicito iye!
Jeremia 15:3 An Rwot, dok atyeko moko kit jami aŋwen maraco ma bityekogi: gibinekogi woko liweŋ ki pala lucwan, gwogi biywayo komgi muto-ni bedo me acamagi, winyo bene gibicamo komgi; ki lee mager me tim doŋ gibimwodogi gityekogi woko liweŋ.
Jeremia 15:4 Dok abimiyo gibedo gin ma miyo ker me lobo ducu gibedo ki lworo, pi gin ma Manace wod pa Kejekia kabaka me Juda yam otimo i Jerucalem.
Jeremia 15:5 “Aŋa ma kica bimako i komwu, wun jo Jerucalem, nyo aŋa kono ma bikumo piwu? Aŋa ma koŋ bilokke cuŋ pi kare malac pi penyo kit macalo wun wutye kwede?
Jeremia 15:6 Wun doŋ wutyeko kwera woko, man Rwot ma owaco, wumedde wubedo ka dok cen kare ducu. Pi meno aye mumiyo aryeyo ciŋa i komwu ci anekowu atyekowu woko; doŋ aol woko ki timo kica botwu.
Jeremia 15:7 I gaŋi ducu ma i lobowu, abedo ka pyetowu ki oderona. Anekowu atyekowu woko, wun jona, pien pe wumedo ki lokke wuweko timo timwu marac-ci.
Jeremia 15:8 Anyayo wel-mon-togi doŋ odoko dwoŋ makato kweyo me dog nam woko. Aneko awobewu woko ma komgi pud tek, dok amiyo megigi gubedo ki can ki arem malit adada. Amiyo bene remcwiny ki lworo madwoŋ opoto i komgi oyotoyot laboŋo galle.
Jeremia 15:9 Dako ma onoŋo onywalo litinone abiro kulu cwinye odem woko; otemo yweyo ci pe romo ywe kadi matidi mo. Dyeceŋ ma en tye iye olokke odoko colpiny; obedo ki lewic ma noŋo cwinye opoŋ woko ki can. Doŋ jo megi mukene ma gudoŋ, abimiyo lukworgi nekogi woko ki pala lucwan, man Rwot ma owaco.”
Jeremia 15:10 Can i wiya! Piŋo maa onywala? Oweko alwenyo, nyo ada dok apyemo ki jo ducu ma i lobo. An cen pe amiyo limma me konyo ŋatti, kun amito magoba iye, dok bene nene pe adeno lim ki bot ŋat mo; ento inoŋo ni dano acel acel tye ka loko lok me cena woko acena.
Jeremia 15:11 Ai Rwot, mi lok ma giloko kun gicena kwede-ni obed kumeno ka ce nene pe atiyo gin ma tye atir i nyimi, dok ka ce nene pe apido kwedi lok wa i kom lukworra i kare ma onoŋo gitye i can dok ki cwercwiny mukato kare.
Jeremia 15:12 Dano twero turo nyonyo, nyonyo ma gikelo ki i lobo ma tye yo tuŋ acam kacel ki mola?
Jeremia 15:13 “Lonyowu kacel ki limwu ma yam wukano abimiyo giyako woko laboŋo wel, pi balwu ducu ma doŋ wutyeko timo ma oromo i lobowu-ni woko liweŋ.
Jeremia 15:14 Abimiyo wubedo opii pa lumerokwu kun wutiyo tic botgi i lobo ma pe wuŋeyo, pien mac doŋ olyel ki i kinigana ma bibedo ka waŋ nakanaka.”
Jeremia 15:15 Mumiyo Jeremia owacci, “Ai Rwot, in iniaŋ dok iŋeyo. Po pira dok ikonya, dok bene myero icul kwor i kom jo ma mito neka woko-ni. Pe myero idi cwinyi i kom jo ma gimito neka woko; myero iŋe bene ni piri omiyo atye ka ciro lok me cac matek.
Jeremia 15:16 Ka yam lokki obino bota, ci acamo ki cwinya matek, lokki olokke odoko gin me yomcwiny bota, dok obedo gin ma yomo cwinya adada; pien an doŋ gilwoŋa a ki nyiŋi, ai Rwot Lubaŋa me mony.
Jeremia 15:17 Yam pe abedo kacel ki jo ma nyero nyero ata pi noŋo yomcwiny me lobo-ni, an kikoma gira cwinya pe obedo yom wacel. Pi tic ma onoŋo in imiya, abedo kena, dok kinigani oketo koma woko.
Jeremia 15:18 Piŋo mono aremma pe gik, ma burra bene doŋ odoko gin ma pe can, okwero gire caŋ woko? In imito ilokke ibed bota calo kulu ma bwolo dano abwola, calo pii ma two woko-ni?”
Jeremia 15:19 Pi meno Rwot owaco kuman ni, “Ka ilokke idwogo bota, ci abigami doki, ci ibicuŋ i nyima kare ducu. Ka ce ibedo ka loko lok maber ma konnye tye, ma pe iloko gin mo ma konnye pe, abiloko in doŋ ibedo ma ka doga. Dano gibilokke gidwogo boti, ento in pe ibilokke idok botgi.
Jeremia 15:20 Doŋ abiketo in ibedo bot lwak man macalo cel gogo me mola ma girumo maber; gin jo-nu gibilwenyo i komi, ento pe gibiloyi ki lweny, pien an atye kwedi abikoki dok abilari, man Rwot ma owaco.
Jeremia 15:21 Abilari woko ki i ciŋ jo maraco, dok abikoki woko ki i ciŋ jo ma tye laboŋo kica.”
Jeremia 16:1 Rwot dok oloko bota owacci,
Jeremia 16:2 “In pe ibinyomo dako mo, dok pe ibibedo ki litino awobe nyo kadi ki litino anyira i kabedo man.
Jeremia 16:3 Pien Rwot owaco lok kuman i kom awobe ki anyira ma ginywalogi i kabedo-ni, dok bene oloko i kom mego ki wego ma gunywalo litino magi i kabedo man ni.
Jeremia 16:4 Two maraco atika binekogi woko. Dano pe bikok pigi, dok bene pe gibiyikogi, ento gibibedo macalo cet dyaŋ muket ata i ŋom; Gibinekogi woko ki pala lucwan, ki kec bene binekogi woko, doŋ komgi muto-ni bidoko cam pa winyo ki lee me tim.”
Jeremia 16:5 Rwot dok owaco kuman ni, “Pe myero idony i ot ka ma dano tye iye ka kumo, pe myero icit ka koko nyo ka kumo pigi; pien doŋ atyeko kwanyo kucca woko ki bot lwak man, man Rwot ma owaco, kadi wa mar mera ma pe lokke ki kicana bene.
Jeremia 16:6 Jo mulony kacel ki lucan gibito i lobo man, ento ŋat mo pe ma biyikogi nyo ma bikok pigi. Ŋat mo bene pe biŋolo kome kekene kun lyelo yer wiye woko pi nyuto can ma tye i cwinye.
Jeremia 16:7 Pe tye ŋat mo ma binywako cam kacel ki dano ma tye ki kumo, wek okwe cwinye pi dano muto ca. Dano mo bene pe bimiyo ginamata mo ma nyuto cwiny me kica bot ŋat ma wonne nyo minne oto.
Jeremia 16:8 Pe myero idony i ot ka ma dano tye ka camo iye karama, me bedo kwedgi kunnu ka cam ki ka mat.
Jeremia 16:9 Rwot me mony ma en Lubaŋa me Icrael owaco kuman ni, Nen, i kabedo man en aye abijuko iye woo me yomcwiny woko matwal ki i waŋwu ma wun bene wuneno, ki i karewu, dwan me oree ki me yomcwiny, dwan lanyom kacel ki dwan nyako ger.
Jeremia 16:10 “Ka doŋ itito lok magi ki lwak man, ce gupenyi ni, ‘Piŋo Rwot kono otimo gin marac macalo man i komwa? Wabalo aŋo? Kit bal aŋo ma waŋ watimo i kom Rwot Lubaŋawa?’
Jeremia 16:11 ci in ibitito botgi ni, ‘Kwarowu yam gubwota woko, man lok ma Rwot owaco, dok gubedo ka lubo kor lubaŋa mogo mukene, gutiyo botgi, gubedo ka worogi bene. Gubwota woko dok bene pe gugwoko cikka.
Jeremia 16:12 Ento wun aye doŋ wutiyo gin marac atika ma kato gin ma yam kwarowu gutimo. Wun ducu wubedo jo ma ŋutwu nwaŋ ki ma kitwu rac, wukwero winyo lokka woko.
Jeremia 16:13 Pi meno abikwanyowu woko ki i lobo man abolowu woko i lobo mukene ma yam wun nyo kadi kwarowu pe guŋeyo. Doŋ ka wutye kunnu en aye wubibedo ka woro lubaŋa mukene-gu dyeceŋ ki dyewor benebene, pe doŋ abinyuto botwu kicana wacel.’
Jeremia 16:14 “Pi meno wunen, kare tye ka bino, man Rwot ma owaco, ma pe dok ŋat mo biwaco ni, ‘Macalo Rwot tye makwo-ni, ma en aye okwanyo waŋ jo Icrael okelowa woko ki i lobo Ejipt,’
Jeremia 16:15 ento wubiwacci, ‘Macalo Rwot tye kwo-ni, ma okelo jo Icrael woko ki i lobo ma yo tuŋ acam, dok ki i lobo ducu ka ma yam en oryemogi gucito iye.’ Pien abikwanyogi adwokogi cen i lobogi kikome ma yam amiyo bot kwarogi.
Jeremia 16:16 “Nen, atye ka cwalo dano mapol, man Rwot ma owaco, ma gibimakogi macalo gimako rec; lacen dok abicwalo jo ma gin ludwar mapol, ma gibidwarogi ki i wi godi-gu ducu kadi ki i wi cere-gu, kadi wa ki i kin got mubar.
Jeremia 16:17 Pien aciko waŋa atye ka neno kitgi ducu; gin pe gukanne ki bota wacel, dok balgi mo ma tye macalo muŋ ma gikano woko ki tuŋ bota pe tye.
Jeremia 16:18 Abiculo waŋ balgi ki bal ma gutimo kiryo, pien gupyedo lobona woko ki cal jogigi ma rom ki kom jo muto-gu, doŋ gupoŋo gipinnya ki timo gin me kwer keken.”
Jeremia 16:19 Ai Rwot, in i tek mera ki cel gogona matek ka ma ariŋo alaro iye i kare me can, rok ducu gibia gibino boti, kun gia ki i agikki lobo, ma giwacci, “Kwarowa yam guleyo gin ma tere pe, lok goba keken, guleyo jami ma konygi pe ma pe gunoŋo iye magoba mo.
Jeremia 16:20 Dano twero tiyo lwak lubaŋa pire kene? Kit gin macalo meno pe lubaŋa wacel.”
Jeremia 16:21 “Pi meno, abimiyo giŋeyo, abimiyo giŋeyo twerona ki tekona kicel keken, ci doŋ gibiŋeyo ni an nyina Rwot.”
Jeremia 17:1 Rwot owacci, “Wun jo Juda, balwu doŋ gicoyo woko ki kalam nyonyo, gigoro woko bene i cwinywu ki kidi dayaman ma lake bit, ki i kom ten keno aŋwen ma tye i kom keno tyerwu,
Jeremia 17:2 en ma miyo litinowu po i kom keno tyerwu ki i kom cal Acera ma jok ma dako ma wucibo i ŋet yadi ducu ma potgi oluk, i wi cere mabocogu,
Jeremia 17:3 ki i wi godi ducu ma tye i dye tim. Lonyowu kacel ki limwu ma yam wukano abimiyo giyako woko, pi balwu ducu ma doŋ wutyeko timo ma oromo i lobowu- ni woko liweŋ.
Jeremia 17:4 Wubikwanyo ciŋwu woko ki i kom gipiny ma yam amiyo botwu, abimiyo wubedo opii pa lumerokwu kun wutiyo tic botgi i lobo ma pe wuŋeyo, pien mac doŋ olyel ki i kinigana ma bibedo ka waŋ nakanaka.”
Jeremia 17:5 Rwot owaco kuman ni, “Ŋat ma keto genne i kom dano giceno woko, ma keto genne i kom kero pa dano, ŋat ma loko cwinye woko ki i kom Rwot.
Jeremia 17:6 En bedo calo yat ma i dye tim aroo, ma pe bineno gin mo maber ka bino. En bibedo mere i kabedo mutwo mubedo kado kado ma gir, mo pe doŋo iye, i kabedo ka ma dano pe bedo iye.
Jeremia 17:7 “Dano ma geno Rwot tye ki gum, ma genne ducu ocuŋ i kom Rwot.
Jeremia 17:8 En bedo calo yat ma gipito i ŋet kulu, ma cwalo lwite donyo woko piny wa i laora kulu. Ka i kare me lyeto ma piny otwo en pe lworo gin mo, pien pote bedo madyak kumeno, dok bene i mwaka ma cen ryeny teretere ma pii pe en pe paro gin mo, dok pe giko nyako nyige.”
Jeremia 17:9 Cwiny dano en aye gin ma bwolo dano ma kato gin mukene-gu ducu, opoŋ ki gin marac adada; aŋa ma twero niaŋ iye?
Jeremia 17:10 “An Rwot aŋiyo tam pa dano dok bene atemo cwiny dano, wek ami bot dano acel acel gin ma lubo kite, dok ma lu bo kit gin ma en otiyo.”
Jeremia 17:11 Macalo ayweri ma coko litino i te bwome ma en kikome pe otoko, ŋat ma noŋo lonyo i yo ma pe atir bene tye kit meno; ka doŋ oteggi inoŋo ni lonyone rwenyo woko, i agikkine en gire doko lamiŋ.
Jeremia 17:12 Kabedowa maleŋ me woro Lubaŋa nen calo kom me deyo adada, ma ocuŋ malo i wi got nia i acakkine.
Jeremia 17:13 Ai Rwot, gen pa jo Icrael ducu tye i komi, jo ducu ma gibwoti woko lewic bimakogi matek; jo ma gilokke giweki woko gibirwenyo woko calo nyiŋ ma gicoyo i apwa, pien gin doŋ gutyeko bwoto Rwot woko, ma en aye waŋ it me pii me kwo.
Jeremia 17:14 Caŋa, ai Rwot, ci abicaŋ woko maber; lara, ci bene abilarre; pien an apako in kare ducu.
Jeremia 17:15 Nen, giwaco bota ni, “Lok pa Rwot tye kwene? wek lokke obin!”
Jeremia 17:16 An pe adiyo in ni myero icwal gin marac, dok bene an pe amito nino me can amita, meno in iŋeyo; gin ma oa ki i doga ducu ma aloko, aloko atyer ka waŋi.
Jeremia 17:17 Pe ibed gin ma kelo lworo bota; in i kalarrena i kare ma noŋo piny rac.
Jeremia 17:18 Wek lewic omak jo ma giketo ayela i koma, ento pe iwek lewic omaka; wek cwinygi aye oballe woko, ento in pe iwek meri cwinya oballe; mi kare ma gin marac myero opot kwede i komgi; tyekgi woko licwic ki nek ma iketo i komgi kiryo!
Jeremia 17:19 Rwot owaco bota kuman ni, “Cit icuŋ i dogcel pa Benjamin, en aye ka ma luker me Juda gidonyo kwede i i gaŋ dok bene yo ma gikato kwede woko; cuŋ bene i dogcel ducu me Jerucalem,
Jeremia 17:20 ci iwac botgi ni, ‘Wuwiny lok pa Rwot, wun luker me Juda, ki jo Juda ducu, ki jo ducu ma gibedo i Jerucalem, ma gidonyo ki i dog gaŋi magi.
Jeremia 17:21 Rwot owaco kuman ni, Ka wumaro kwo myero pe wutiŋ ter i ceŋ cabit; dok pe myero wukel gin mo kun wuwok ki i dog gaŋi ducu me Jerucalem.
Jeremia 17:22 Dok bene pe myero wutiŋ ter ki i otwu i ceŋ cabit, dok pe wuti tic mo, ento myero wukwer nino me cabit obed maleŋ kit macalo yam aciko ki kwarowu.
Jeremia 17:23 Ento kwarowu yam pe guwinyo, gujiŋo ŋutgi obedo matek, pe guciko itgi ka winyo lokka, wek pe guwiny dok gugam pwony ma mera.
Jeremia 17:24 “ ‘Ento ka wuwinyo lokka, man Rwot ma owaco, ma pe wukelo ter mo ki i dogcel ducu me gaŋ man i ceŋ cabit, ento kun wukwero ceŋ cabit bedo nino maleŋ ma pe wutiyo tic mo i nino meno,
Jeremia 17:25 doŋ lukerwu ki rwodiwu bidonyo ki i dogcel me Jerucalem ma gibedo i wi komker pa Daudi. Gin ki rwodigi ducu kacel ki jo Juda ki jo Jerucalem, gibiriŋo ki gadigadi ki aguragura, doŋ meno bimiyo gaŋ me Jerucalem bipoŋ ki lwak dano mapol matwal.
Jeremia 17:26 Dano gibia gibino ki i gaŋi me Juda ki i gaŋi matitino ma i ŋet Jerucalem; gibibino ki i lobo pa Benjamin, ki i lobo me Cepela, ki i lobo ma obedo godigodi, dok bene gibia gibino ki i Negeb, kun gikelo gityer me gitum awaŋa, gityer me moko kwoŋ, ki odok luban, dok gikelo gityer me pwoc bene i ot pa Rwot.
Jeremia 17:27 Ento ka wun pe wuwinyo lokka me kwero ceŋ cabit wek obed maleŋ, dok ni pe wutiŋ ter mo wudony kwede ki i dogcel me Jerucalem i ceŋ cabit, ci abimiyo mac lyel i dogcelle ducu biwaŋo odi madoŋo me Jerucalerri woko ducu ma macce pe doŋ gibiromo nekone matwal.’ ”
Jeremia 18:1 Rwot owacca ni,
Jeremia 18:2 “A malo icit i ot pa lwacwe agulu, ci abimiyo iwinyo lokka ki kunnu.”
Jeremia 18:3 Ci aa acito i ot pa lacwe agulu, ci anoŋo en tye ka cweyo agulune i kom lawala.
Jeremia 18:4 Ci lobo agulu ma onoŋo lacwe agulu tye ka cweyone-ni oballe woko ki i ciŋe, ci ni ber bote me atima.
Jeremia 18:5 Rwot dok owaco bota ni,
Jeremia 18:6 “Wun jo me ot pa Icrael, pe atwero tiyo i komwu gin ma lacwe agulu otiyo-ni? Man Rwot ma owaco. Nen, wun jo Icrael bene wutye i ciŋa macalo lobo ma tye i cin lacwe agulu.
Jeremia 18:7 Ka ce i kare mo awaco pi rok mo ni abiputo dok aturo woko ci abityeko woko,
Jeremia 18:8 ka ce doŋ rok meno ma aloko pire-ni olokke oweko timo gin marac, ci abinut pi gin marac ma onoŋo atamo ni atimo i kome ca.
Jeremia 18:9 Dok bene ka ce onoŋo awacci abipito nyo agero rok nyo ker mo-ni,
Jeremia 18:10 ce rok meno okwero winyo doga olokke ka timo gin marac, ci abiloko tamma i kom gin maber ma onoŋo awaco ni abitimo botgi-ni.
Jeremia 18:11 Kombeddi doŋ itit bot jo Juda ki jo ma bedo i Jerucalem ni, ‘Rwot owaco kuman ni, Nen, atye ki yub marac piwu dok ayubbe me keto can i komwu. Wulokke wudwog cen, ŋat acel acel owek kit marac woko, dok oyub kite kun tiyo gin ma tye atir.’
Jeremia 18:12 “Ento gin gigamo ni, ‘Lokke pe konyo! Wabilubo yub ma waŋ kikomwa aye wayubo, ki ŋat acel acel bene bitiyo gin ducu ma oporo rac cwinye ma nwan-ni.’
Jeremia 18:13 “Mumiyo Rwot owaco kuman ni, Ka imito koŋ ipeny i kin lurok, aŋa ma yam owinyo lok mo ma cal ki man? Jo Icrael ma amaro doŋ gutimo gin marac adada.
Jeremia 18:14 Pee me Lebanon mo no twero weko lacol got me Cirion? Kulu ma piine nie ma mol a ki i wi godi twero two woko liweŋ?
Jeremia 18:15 Ento jona doŋ wigi otyeko wil woko i koma; gibedo ka wano odok eceta bot cal lubaŋa-gu; gubedo ka yokke atata i kit me wot megi, pe gulubo yo macon, dok bene guwoto ki i yo mogo ma wok ki cen, pe guwoto ki i yo gudo,
Jeremia 18:16 ma guloko lobogi odoko gin ma miyo lworo bot dano, ma bibedo gin ma gijwat pire kun gicayo nakanaka. Jo ducu ma gibikato ki i ka ŋete gibibedo ki ur madit twatwal kun giyeŋo wigi.
Jeremia 18:17 Abikeyo jona woko i nyim lukworgi, calo apwa ma yamo wokceŋ tye ka tiŋone. Abiloko ŋeya woko botgi; pe abikonyogi ka can opoto komgi.”
Jeremia 18:18 Lacen lwak guwacci, “Wubin wapiru lok i kom Jeremia! Kare ducu wabibedo ki ajwagi ma giromo pwonyowa, ki luryeko bene ma gibibedo ka miyo botwa tam, dok wabibedo ki lunebi ma gimedde anyim ki tito lok pa Lubaŋa, Wubin, wek wakelu lok me pido i kome, doŋ bene wagiku keto cwinywa i lok ducu ma en owaco-gu.”
Jeremia 18:19 Pi meno Jeremia olego Lubaŋa, kun wacci, “Rwot, winy lok ma atye ka wacone- ni, ki dok bene iwiny lok ma lukworra gitye ka lokone i koma.
Jeremia 18:20 Gin marac mono aye giculo ki ŋat ma timo gin maber? Doŋ gutyeko kwinyo bur woko ni myero apot iye. Koŋ ipo kit macalo abino kwede i nyimi kun apido pigi ma aloko lok maber, wek ikwany akemoni woko ki i komgi.
Jeremia 18:21 Pi meno doŋ imi kec onek litinogi otyekgi woko; dok bene wek ginekgi woko i lweny ki pala lucwan. Wek mongi gudoŋ laboŋo litino dok bene gudok mon-to. Wek two gemo aye onek coggi otyekgi woko, ki awobegi bene myero ginekgi woko i mony ki pala lucwan.
Jeremia 18:22 Cwal dul mony atura me yako gaŋigi woko, wek guwo ki koko ma kelo lworo. Doŋ gutyeko kwinyo bur woko wek apot iye, dok guciko owic woko wek amok iye.
Jeremia 18:23 Ento in, ai Rwot, iŋeyo kit macalo gipiro kwede lok i koma wek gineka woko. Pe itimgi ki ca pi gin marac ma gitimo, pe bene ijwa balgi woko matwal ki i nyimi. Wek gibed ka loyogi kumeno i nyimi; ti kwedgi i kare ma noŋo kiniga omaki.”
Jeremia 19:1 Rwot owaco kuman ni, “Cit iciwil abino ma lacwe agulu ocweyo, kwany ludoŋo pa lwak ki ajwagi ma guteggi ma doŋ guri i dog tic icit kwedgi,
Jeremia 19:2 ci wucit wukat woko wa i nota pa wod pa Kinom, kun wudonyo ki i dogcel me Labaltak, ci icitit lok ma awaco boti-ni ducu ki kunnu.
Jeremia 19:3 Ibiwacci, ‘Wuwiny lok pa Rwot, wun luker me Juda ki jo ma bedo i Jerucalem. Rwot me mony ma en Lubaŋa pa Icrael owaco kuman ni, Nen, atye ka kelo gin marac twatwal i kom kabedo man, mi yo dano ducu ma gibiwinyo pire itgi bibedo ka wo awoya liwaŋ waŋ.
Jeremia 19:4 Abitimo gin ma kit man pien dano gutyeko bwota woko, dok bene gubalo kabedo man woko, kun giwaŋo iye odok eceta bot lwak lubaŋa mukene ma gin kikomgi nyo kwarogi kadi ki luker me Juda onoŋo yam pe guŋeyo. Gupoŋo kabedo man woko ki remo pa jo ma gipe ki bal,
